                  </div>
                </details>

      <div id="readme" class="Box-body readme blob js-code-block-container p-5 p-xl-6 gist-border-0">
    <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><h1><a id="user-content-1mysql环境" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#1mysql环境"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>1.MySQL环境</h1>
<h2><a id="user-content-11环境安装" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#11环境安装"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>1.1.环境安装</h2>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 查看Linux服务器上是否安装过MySQL</span>
rpm -qa <span class="pl-k">|</span> grep -i mysql <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 查询出所有mysql依赖包</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 1、拉取镜像</span>
docker pull mysql:5.7

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 2、创建实例并启动</span>
docker run -p 3306:3306 --name mysql \
-v /root/mysql/log:/var/log/mysql \
-v /root/mysql/data:/var/lib/mysql \
-v /root/mysql/conf:/etc/mysql \
-e MYSQL_ROOT_PASSWORD=333 \
-d mysql:5.7

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 3、mysql配置 /root/mysql/conf/my.conf</span>
[client]
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>mysqlde utf8字符集默认为3位的，不支持emoji表情及部分不常见的汉字，故推荐使用utf8mb4</span>
default-character-set=utf8

[mysql]
default-character-set=utf8

[mysqld]
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>设置client连接mysql时的字符集,防止乱码</span>
init_connect=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>SET collation_connection = utf8_general_ci<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
init_connect=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>SET NAMES utf8<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>数据库默认字符集</span>
character-set-server=utf8

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>数据库字符集对应一些排序等规则，注意要和character-set-server对应</span>
collation-server=utf8_general_ci

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 跳过mysql程序起动时的字符参数设置 ，使用服务器端字符集设置</span>
skip-character-set-client-handshake

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 禁止MySQL对外部连接进行DNS解析，使用这一选项可以消除MySQL进行DNS解析的时间。但需要注意，如果开启该选项，则所有远程主机连接授权都要使用IP地址方式，否则MySQL将无法正常处理连接请求！</span>
skip-name-resolve

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 4、重启mysql容器</span>
docker restart mysql

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 5、进入到mysql容器</span>
docker <span class="pl-c1">exec</span> -it mysql /bin/bash

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 6、查看修改的配置文件</span>
cat /etc/mysql/my.conf</pre></div>
<h2><a id="user-content-12安装位置" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#12安装位置"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>1.2.安装位置</h2>
<p><code>Docker</code>容器就是一个小型的<code>Linux</code>环境，进入到<code>MySQL</code>容器中。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>docker <span class="pl-c1">exec</span> -it mysql /bin/bash</pre></div>
<p><code>Linux</code>环境下<code>MySQL</code>的安装目录。</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>路径</th>
<th>解释</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>/var/lib/mysql</code></td>
<td>MySQL数据库文件存放位置</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>/usr/share/mysql</code></td>
<td>错误消息和字符集文件配置</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>/usr/bin</code></td>
<td>客户端程序和脚本</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>/etc/init.d/mysql</code></td>
<td>启停脚本相关</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h2><a id="user-content-13修改字符集" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#13修改字符集"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>1.3.修改字符集</h2>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 1、进入到mysql数据库并查看字符集</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> show variables like 'character%';</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> show variables like '%char%';</span>

mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> show variables like <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>character%<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span>
+--------------------------+----------------------------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Variable_name            <span class="pl-k">|</span> Value                      <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+--------------------------+----------------------------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> character_set_client     <span class="pl-k">|</span> utf8                       <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> character_set_connection <span class="pl-k">|</span> utf8                       <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> character_set_database   <span class="pl-k">|</span> utf8                       <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> character_set_filesystem <span class="pl-k">|</span> binary                     <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> character_set_results    <span class="pl-k">|</span> utf8                       <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> character_set_server     <span class="pl-k">|</span> utf8                       <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> character_set_system     <span class="pl-k">|</span> utf8                       <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> character_sets_dir       <span class="pl-k">|</span> /usr/share/mysql/charsets/ <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+--------------------------+----------------------------+
8 rows <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-c1">set</span> (0.00 sec)

mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> show variables like <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>%char%<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span>
+--------------------------+----------------------------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Variable_name            <span class="pl-k">|</span> Value                      <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+--------------------------+----------------------------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> character_set_client     <span class="pl-k">|</span> utf8                       <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> character_set_connection <span class="pl-k">|</span> utf8                       <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> character_set_database   <span class="pl-k">|</span> utf8                       <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> character_set_filesystem <span class="pl-k">|</span> binary                     <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> character_set_results    <span class="pl-k">|</span> utf8                       <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> character_set_server     <span class="pl-k">|</span> utf8                       <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> character_set_system     <span class="pl-k">|</span> utf8                       <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> character_sets_dir       <span class="pl-k">|</span> /usr/share/mysql/charsets/ <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+--------------------------+----------------------------+
8 rows <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-c1">set</span> (0.01 sec)</pre></div>
<p><code>MySQL5.7</code>配置文件位置是<code>/etc/my.cnf</code>或者<code>/etc/mysql/my.cnf</code>，如果字符集不是<code>utf-8</code>直接进入配置文件修改即可。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>[client]
default-character-set=utf8

[mysql]
default-character-set=utf8

[mysqld]
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 设置client连接mysql时的字符集,防止乱码</span>
init_connect=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>SET NAMES utf8<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
init_connect=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>SET collation_connection = utf8_general_ci<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 数据库默认字符集</span>
character-set-server=utf8

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>数据库字符集对应一些排序等规则，注意要和character-set-server对应</span>
collation-server=utf8_general_ci

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 跳过mysql程序起动时的字符参数设置 ，使用服务器端字符集设置</span>
skip-character-set-client-handshake

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 禁止MySQL对外部连接进行DNS解析，使用这一选项可以消除MySQL进行DNS解析的时间。但需要注意，如果开启该选项，则所有远程主机连接授权都要使用IP地址方式，否则MySQL将无法正常处理连接请求！</span>
skip-name-resolve</pre></div>
<p><strong>注意：安装<code>MySQL</code>完毕之后，第一件事就是修改字符集编码。</strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-14配置文件" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#14配置文件"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>1.4.配置文件</h2>
<p><strong><code>MySQL</code>配置文件讲解：<a href="https://www.cnblogs.com/gaoyuechen/p/10273102.html" rel="nofollow">https://www.cnblogs.com/gaoyuechen/p/10273102.html</a></strong></p>
<p>1、二进制日志<code>log-bin</code>：主从复制。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> my,cnf</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 开启mysql binlog功能</span>
log-bin=mysql-bin</pre></div>
<p>2、错误日志<code>log-error</code>：默认是关闭的，记录严重的警告和错误信息，每次启动和关闭的详细信息等。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> my,cnf</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 数据库错误日志文件</span>
log-error = error.log</pre></div>
<p>3、查询日志<code>log</code>：默认关闭，记录查询的<code>sql</code>语句，如果开启会降低<code>MySQL</code>整体的性能，因为记录日志需要消耗系统资源。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> my,cnf</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 慢查询sql日志设置</span>
slow_query_log = 1
slow_query_log_file = slow.log</pre></div>
<p>4、数据文件。</p>
<ul>
<li><code>frm文件</code>：存放表结构。</li>
<li><code>myd</code>文件：存放表数据。</li>
<li><code>myi</code>文件：存放表索引。</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> mysql5.7 使用.frm文件来存储表结构</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 使用 .ibd文件来存储表索引和表数据</span>
-rw-r-----  1 mysql mysql   8988 Jun 25 09:31 pms_category.frm
-rw-r-----  1 mysql mysql 245760 Jul 21 10:01 pms_category.ibd</pre></div>
<p><code>MySQL5.7</code>的<code>Innodb</code>存储引擎可将所有数据存放于<code>ibdata*</code>的共享表空间，也可将每张表存放于独立的<code>.ibd</code>文件的独立表空间。
共享表空间以及独立表空间都是针对数据的存储方式而言的。</p>
<ul>
<li>共享表空间: 某一个数据库的所有的表数据，索引文件全部放在一个文件中，默认这个共享表空间的文件路径在<code>data</code>目录下。 默认的文件名为<code>:ibdata1</code> 初始化为<code>10M</code>。</li>
<li>独立表空间: 每一个表都将会生成以独立的文件方式来进行存储，每一个表都有一个<code>.frm</code>表描述文件，还有一个<code>.ibd</code>文件。 其中这个文件包括了单独一个表的数据内容以及索引内容，默认情况下它的存储位置也是在表的位置之中。在配置文件<code>my.cnf</code>中设置： <code>innodb_file_per_table</code>。</li>
</ul>
<h1><a id="user-content-2mysql逻辑架构" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#2mysql逻辑架构"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>2.MySQL逻辑架构</h1>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/93724a49f5bba4e13c129caecaa62929be096861cf63edc807c8f1bc5db86699/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e2e6e65742f32303138303833313137333931313939373f77617465726d61726b2f322f746578742f6148523063484d364c7939696247396e4c6d4e7a5a473475626d56304c337066636e6c6862673d3d2f666f6e742f3561364c354c32542f666f6e7473697a652f3430302f66696c6c2f49304a42516b46434d413d3d2f646973736f6c76652f3730"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/93724a49f5bba4e13c129caecaa62929be096861cf63edc807c8f1bc5db86699/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e2e6e65742f32303138303833313137333931313939373f77617465726d61726b2f322f746578742f6148523063484d364c7939696247396e4c6d4e7a5a473475626d56304c337066636e6c6862673d3d2f666f6e742f3561364c354c32542f666f6e7473697a652f3430302f66696c6c2f49304a42516b46434d413d3d2f646973736f6c76652f3730" alt="MySQL逻辑架构" data-canonical-src="https://img-blog.csdn.net/20180831173911997?watermark/2/text/aHR0cHM6Ly9ibG9nLmNzZG4ubmV0L3pfcnlhbg==/font/5a6L5L2T/fontsize/400/fill/I0JBQkFCMA==/dissolve/70" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><code>Connectors</code>：指的是不同语言中与SQL的交互。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>Connection Pool</code>：管理缓冲用户连接，线程处理等需要缓存的需求。<strong>MySQL数据库的连接层。</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code> Management Serveices &amp; Utilities</code>：系统管理和控制工具。备份、安全、复制、集群等等。。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>SQL Interface</code>：接受用户的SQL命令，并且返回用户需要查询的结果。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>Parser</code>：SQL语句解析器。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>Optimizer</code>：查询优化器，SQL语句在查询之前会使用查询优化器对查询进行优化。<strong>就是优化客户端请求query</strong>，根据客户端请求的 query 语句，和数据库中的一些统计信息，在一系列算法的基础上进行分析，得出一个最优的策略，告诉后面的程序如何取得这个 query 语句的结果。<strong>For Example</strong>： <code>select uid,name from user where gender = 1;</code>这个<code>select </code>查询先根据<code>where </code>语句进行选取，而不是先将表全部查询出来以后再进行<code>gender</code>过滤；然后根据<code>uid</code>和<code>name</code>进行属性投影，而不是将属性全部取出以后再进行过滤。最后将这两个查询条件联接起来生成最终查询结果。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>Caches &amp; Buffers</code>：查询缓存。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>Pluggable Storage Engines</code>：<strong>存储引擎接口。MySQL区别于其他数据库的最重要的特点就是其插件式的表存储引擎(注意：存储引擎是基于表的，而不是数据库)。</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>File System</code>：数据落地到磁盘上，就是文件的存储。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>MySQL数据库和其他数据库相比，MySQL有点与众不同，主要体现在存储引擎的架构上，<strong>插件式的存储引擎架构将查询处理和其他的系统任务以及数据的存储提取相分离</strong>。这种架构可以根据业务的需求和实际需求选择合适的存储引擎。</p>
<blockquote>
<p>逻辑架构分层</p>
</blockquote>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/6c2ee2b60cb88f90523e81023b59dfbb550b13dfa3f0472c89228e85e038fc73/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830313136353235323531302e706e673f782d6f73732d70726f636573733d696d6167652f77617465726d61726b2c747970655f5a6d46755a33706f5a57356e6147567064476b2c736861646f775f31302c746578745f6148523063484d364c7939696247396e4c6d4e7a5a473475626d56304c314a796157356e6231383d2c73697a655f31362c636f6c6f725f4646464646462c745f3730"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/6c2ee2b60cb88f90523e81023b59dfbb550b13dfa3f0472c89228e85e038fc73/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830313136353235323531302e706e673f782d6f73732d70726f636573733d696d6167652f77617465726d61726b2c747970655f5a6d46755a33706f5a57356e6147567064476b2c736861646f775f31302c746578745f6148523063484d364c7939696247396e4c6d4e7a5a473475626d56304c314a796157356e6231383d2c73697a655f31362c636f6c6f725f4646464646462c745f3730" alt="MySQL逻辑架构" data-canonical-src="https://img-blog.csdnimg.cn/20200801165252510.png?x-oss-process=image/watermark,type_ZmFuZ3poZW5naGVpdGk,shadow_10,text_aHR0cHM6Ly9ibG9nLmNzZG4ubmV0L1JyaW5nb18=,size_16,color_FFFFFF,t_70" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>连接层：最上层是一些客户端和连接服务，包含本地sock通信和大多数基于客户端/服务端工具实现的类似于<code>tcp/ip</code>的通信。主要完成一些类似于连接处理、授权认证、及相关的安全方案。在该层上引入了线程池的概念，为通过认证安全接入的客户端提供线程。同样在该层上可以实现基于<code>SSL</code>的安全链接。服务器也会为安全接入的每个客户端验证它所具有的操作权限。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>服务层：MySQL的核心服务功能层，该层是MySQL的核心，包括查询缓存，解析器，解析树，预处理器，查询优化器。主要进行查询解析、分析、查询缓存、内置函数、存储过程、触发器、视图等，select操作会先检查是否命中查询缓存，命中则直接返回缓存数据，否则解析查询并创建对应的解析树。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>引擎层：存储引擎层，存储引擎真正的负责了MySQL中数据的存储和提取，服务器通过API与存储引擎进行通信。不同的存储引擎具有的功能不同，这样我们可以根据自己的实际需要进行选取。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>存储层：数据存储层，主要是将数据存储在运行于裸设备的文件系统之上，并完成与存储引擎的交互。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1><a id="user-content-3存储引擎" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#3存储引擎"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>3.存储引擎</h1>
<p><code>show engines;</code>命令查看MySQL5.7支持的存储引擎。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> show engines<span class="pl-k">;</span></pre></div>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/1c5a3b84879ec1a2e71d71f98ba620f9cc241d7ac21cede9c4ff8d380b178161/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830313137303434323432382e706e673f782d6f73732d70726f636573733d696d6167652f77617465726d61726b2c747970655f5a6d46755a33706f5a57356e6147567064476b2c736861646f775f31302c746578745f6148523063484d364c7939696247396e4c6d4e7a5a473475626d56304c314a796157356e6231383d2c73697a655f31362c636f6c6f725f4646464646462c745f3730"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/1c5a3b84879ec1a2e71d71f98ba620f9cc241d7ac21cede9c4ff8d380b178161/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830313137303434323432382e706e673f782d6f73732d70726f636573733d696d6167652f77617465726d61726b2c747970655f5a6d46755a33706f5a57356e6147567064476b2c736861646f775f31302c746578745f6148523063484d364c7939696247396e4c6d4e7a5a473475626d56304c314a796157356e6231383d2c73697a655f31362c636f6c6f725f4646464646462c745f3730" alt="存储引擎" data-canonical-src="https://img-blog.csdnimg.cn/20200801170442428.png?x-oss-process=image/watermark,type_ZmFuZ3poZW5naGVpdGk,shadow_10,text_aHR0cHM6Ly9ibG9nLmNzZG4ubmV0L1JyaW5nb18=,size_16,color_FFFFFF,t_70" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p><code>show variables like 'default_storage_engine%';</code>查看当前数据库正在使用的存储引擎。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> show variables like <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>default_storage_engine%<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span>
+------------------------+--------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Variable_name          <span class="pl-k">|</span> Value  <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+------------------------+--------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> default_storage_engine <span class="pl-k">|</span> InnoDB <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+------------------------+--------+
1 row <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-c1">set</span> (0.01 sec)</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>InnoDB和MyISAM对比</p>
</blockquote>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="left">对比项</th>
<th align="center">MyISAM</th>
<th align="center">InnoDB</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="left">主外键</td>
<td align="center">不支持</td>
<td align="center">支持</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">事务</td>
<td align="center">不支持</td>
<td align="center">支持</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">行表锁</td>
<td align="center">表锁，即使操作一条记录也会锁住整张表，<strong>不适合高并发操作</strong></td>
<td align="center">行锁，操作时只锁某一行，不对其他行有影响，<strong>适合高并发操作</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">缓存</td>
<td align="center">只缓存索引，不缓存真实数据</td>
<td align="center">不仅缓存索引还要缓存真实数据，対内存要求较高，而且内存大小対性能有决定性影响</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">表空间</td>
<td align="center">小</td>
<td align="center">大</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">关注点</td>
<td align="center">性能</td>
<td align="center">事务</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">默认安装</td>
<td align="center">Y</td>
<td align="center">Y</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h1><a id="user-content-4sql性能下降的原因" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#4sql性能下降的原因"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>4.SQL性能下降的原因</h1>
<ul>
<li>查询语句写的差。</li>
<li>索引失效：索引建了，但是没有用上。</li>
<li>关联 查询太多<code>join</code>（设计缺陷或者不得已的需求）。</li>
<li>服务器调优以及各个参数的设置（缓冲、线程数等）。</li>
</ul>
<h1><a id="user-content-5sql执行顺序" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#5sql执行顺序"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>5.SQL执行顺序</h1>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-k">select</span>              <span class="pl-smi">#</span> 5
	... 
from                <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 1</span>
	... 
where               <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 2</span>
	.... 
group by            <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 3</span>
	... 
having              <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 4</span>
	... 
order by            <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 6</span>
	... 
limit               <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 7</span>
	[offset]</pre></div>
<h1><a id="user-content-6七种join理论" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#6七种join理论"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>6.七种JOIN理论</h1>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/86ddd9cb519bf327ca485e638dd17d8ec15e10778a6b1d85b7c6dfa54d553df1/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830313231323031313535392e6a70673f782d6f73732d70726f636573733d696d6167652f77617465726d61726b2c747970655f5a6d46755a33706f5a57356e6147567064476b2c736861646f775f31302c746578745f6148523063484d364c7939696247396e4c6d4e7a5a473475626d56304c314a796157356e6231383d2c73697a655f31362c636f6c6f725f4646464646462c745f3730"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/86ddd9cb519bf327ca485e638dd17d8ec15e10778a6b1d85b7c6dfa54d553df1/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830313231323031313535392e6a70673f782d6f73732d70726f636573733d696d6167652f77617465726d61726b2c747970655f5a6d46755a33706f5a57356e6147567064476b2c736861646f775f31302c746578745f6148523063484d364c7939696247396e4c6d4e7a5a473475626d56304c314a796157356e6231383d2c73697a655f31362c636f6c6f725f4646464646462c745f3730" alt="七种JOIN理论" data-canonical-src="https://img-blog.csdnimg.cn/20200801212011559.jpg?x-oss-process=image/watermark,type_ZmFuZ3poZW5naGVpdGk,shadow_10,text_aHR0cHM6Ly9ibG9nLmNzZG4ubmV0L1JyaW5nb18=,size_16,color_FFFFFF,t_70" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 1 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>select_list<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> TableA A <span class="pl-k">LEFT JOIN</span> TableB B <span class="pl-k">ON</span> <span class="pl-c1">A</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">B</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 2 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>select_list<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> TableA A <span class="pl-k">RIGHT JOIN</span> TableB B <span class="pl-k">ON</span> <span class="pl-c1">A</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">B</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 3 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>select_list<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> TableA A <span class="pl-k">INNER JOIN</span> TableB B <span class="pl-k">ON</span> <span class="pl-c1">A</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">B</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 4 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>select_list<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> TableA A <span class="pl-k">LEFT JOIN</span> TableB B <span class="pl-k">ON</span> <span class="pl-c1">A</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">B</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-c1">B</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span> IS <span class="pl-k">NULL</span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 5 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>select_list<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> TableA A <span class="pl-k">RIGHT JOIN</span> TableB B <span class="pl-k">ON</span> <span class="pl-c1">A</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">B</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-c1">A</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span> IS <span class="pl-k">NULL</span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 6 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>select_list<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> TableA A FULL OUTER <span class="pl-k">JOIN</span> TableB B <span class="pl-k">ON</span> <span class="pl-c1">A</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">B</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span>;
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> MySQL不支持FULL OUTER JOIN这种语法 可以改成 1+2 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>select_list<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> TableA A <span class="pl-k">LEFT JOIN</span> TableB B <span class="pl-k">ON</span> <span class="pl-c1">A</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">B</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span>
<span class="pl-k">UNION</span>
<span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>select_list<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> TableA A <span class="pl-k">RIGHT JOIN</span> TableB B <span class="pl-k">ON</span> <span class="pl-c1">A</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">B</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 7 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>select_list<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> TableA A FULL OUTER <span class="pl-k">JOIN</span> TableB B <span class="pl-k">ON</span> <span class="pl-c1">A</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">B</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-c1">A</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span> IS <span class="pl-k">NULL</span> <span class="pl-k">OR</span> <span class="pl-c1">B</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span> IS <span class="pl-k">NULL</span>;
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> MySQL不支持FULL OUTER JOIN这种语法 可以改成 4+5 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>select_list<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> TableA A <span class="pl-k">LEFT JOIN</span> TableB B <span class="pl-k">ON</span> <span class="pl-c1">A</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">B</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-c1">B</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span> IS <span class="pl-k">NULL</span>;
<span class="pl-k">UNION</span>
<span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>select_list<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> TableA A <span class="pl-k">RIGHT JOIN</span> TableB B <span class="pl-k">ON</span> <span class="pl-c1">A</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">B</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-c1">A</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Key</span> IS <span class="pl-k">NULL</span>;</pre></div>
<h1><a id="user-content-7索引" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#7索引"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>7.索引</h1>
<h2><a id="user-content-71索引简介" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#71索引简介"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>7.1.索引简介</h2>
<blockquote>
<p>索引是什么？</p>
</blockquote>
<p>MySQL官方对索引的定义为：<strong>索引（INDEX）是帮助MySQL高效获取数据的数据结果。</strong></p>
<p>从而可以获得索引的本质：<strong>索引是排好序的快速查找数据结构。</strong></p>
<p>索引的目的在于提高查询效率，可以类比字典的目录。如果要查<code>mysql</code>这个这个单词，我们肯定要先定位到<code>m</code>字母，然后从上往下找<code>y</code>字母，再找剩下的<code>sql</code>。如果没有索引，那么可能需要<code>a---z</code>，这样全字典扫描，如果我想找<code>Java</code>开头的单词呢？如果我想找<code>Oracle</code>开头的单词呢？？？</p>
<p><strong>重点：索引会影响到MySQL查找(WHERE的查询条件)和排序(ORDER BY)两大功能！</strong></p>
<p><strong>除了数据本身之外，数据库还维护着一个满足特定查找算法的数据结构，这些数据结构以某种方式指向数据，这样就可以在这些数据结构的基础上实现高级查找算法，这种数据结构就是索引。</strong></p>
<p>一般来说，索引本身也很大，不可能全部存储在内存中，因此索引往往以索引文件的形式存储在磁盘上。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Linux下查看磁盘空间命令 df -h </span>
[root@Ringo <span class="pl-k">~</span>]<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> df -h</span>
Filesystem      Size  Used Avail Use% Mounted on
/dev/vda1        40G   16G   23G  41% /
devtmpfs        911M     0  911M   0% /dev
tmpfs           920M     0  920M   0% /dev/shm
tmpfs           920M  480K  920M   1% /run
tmpfs           920M     0  920M   0% /sys/fs/cgroup
overlay          40G   16G   23G  41% </pre></div>
<p>我们平时所说的索引，如果没有特别指明，都是指B树（多路搜索树，并不一定是二叉的）结构组织的索引。其中聚集索引，次要索引，覆盖索引，复合索引，前缀索引，唯一索引默认都是使用B+树索引，统称索引。当然，除了B+树这种数据结构的索引之外，还有哈希索引（Hash Index）等。</p>
<blockquote>
<p>索引的优势和劣势</p>
</blockquote>
<p>优势：</p>
<ul>
<li>查找：类似大学图书馆的书目索引，提高数据检索的效率，降低数据库的IO成本。</li>
<li>排序：通过索引対数据进行排序，降低数据排序的成本，降低了CPU的消耗。</li>
</ul>
<p>劣势：</p>
<ul>
<li>实际上索引也是一张表，该表保存了主键与索引字段，并指向实体表的记录，所以索引列也是要占用空间的。</li>
<li>虽然索引大大提高了查询速度，但是同时会降低表的更新速度，例如对表频繁的进行<code>INSERT</code>、<code>UPDATE</code>和<code>DELETE</code>。因为更新表的时候，MySQL不仅要保存数据，还要保存一下索引文件每次更新添加的索引列的字段，都会调整因为更新所带来的键值变化后的索引信息。</li>
<li>索引只是提高效率的一个因素，如果MySQL有大数据量的表，就需要花时间研究建立最优秀的索引。</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-72mysql索引分类" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#72mysql索引分类"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>7.2.MySQL索引分类</h2>
<p>索引分类：</p>
<ul>
<li>单值索引：一个索引只包含单个列，一个表可以有多个单列索引。</li>
<li>唯一索引：索引列的值必须唯一，但是允许空值。</li>
<li>复合索引：一个索引包含多个字段。</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>建议：一张表建的索引最好不要超过5个！</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 基本语法 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 1、创建索引 [UNIQUE]可以省略<span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 如果只写一个字段就是单值索引，写多个字段就是复合索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
CREATE [UNIQUE] INDEX indexName <span class="pl-k">ON</span> tabName(columnName(length));

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 2、删除索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">DROP</span> <span class="pl-k">INDEX</span> [indexName] <span class="pl-k">ON</span> tabName;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 3、查看索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 加上\G就可以以列的形式查看了 不加\G就是以表的形式查看 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
SHOW INDEX <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> tabName \G;</pre></div>
<p>使用<code>ALTER</code>命令来为数据表添加索引</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 1、该语句添加一个主键，这意味着索引值必须是唯一的，并且不能为NULL <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">ALTER</span> <span class="pl-k">TABLE</span> tabName ADD <span class="pl-k">PRIMARY KEY</span>(column_list);

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 2、该语句创建索引的键值必须是唯一的(除了NULL之外，NULL可能会出现多次) <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">ALTER</span> <span class="pl-k">TABLE</span> tabName ADD UNIQUE indexName(column_list);

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 3、该语句创建普通索引，索引值可以出现多次 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">ALTER</span> <span class="pl-k">TABLE</span> tabName ADD INDEX indexName(column_list);

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 4、该语句指定了索引为FULLTEXT，用于全文检索 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">ALTER</span> <span class="pl-k">TABLE</span> tabName ADD FULLTEXT indexName(column_list);</pre></div>
<h2><a id="user-content-73mysql索引数据结构" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#73mysql索引数据结构"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>7.3MySQL索引数据结构</h2>
<p>索引数据结构：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>BTree</code>索引。</li>
<li><code>Hash</code>索引。</li>
<li><code>Full-text</code>全文索引。</li>
<li><code>R-Tree</code>索引。</li>
</ul>
<p><code>BTree</code>索引检索原理：</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/585e16bba5e6911f7d81728ab9731894fd6631963a028f79d6f327d50109b42d/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830313233333133343933312e706e673f782d6f73732d70726f636573733d696d6167652f77617465726d61726b2c747970655f5a6d46755a33706f5a57356e6147567064476b2c736861646f775f31302c746578745f6148523063484d364c7939696247396e4c6d4e7a5a473475626d56304c314a796157356e6231383d2c73697a655f31362c636f6c6f725f4646464646462c745f3730"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/585e16bba5e6911f7d81728ab9731894fd6631963a028f79d6f327d50109b42d/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830313233333133343933312e706e673f782d6f73732d70726f636573733d696d6167652f77617465726d61726b2c747970655f5a6d46755a33706f5a57356e6147567064476b2c736861646f775f31302c746578745f6148523063484d364c7939696247396e4c6d4e7a5a473475626d56304c314a796157356e6231383d2c73697a655f31362c636f6c6f725f4646464646462c745f3730" alt="BTree" data-canonical-src="https://img-blog.csdnimg.cn/20200801233134931.png?x-oss-process=image/watermark,type_ZmFuZ3poZW5naGVpdGk,shadow_10,text_aHR0cHM6Ly9ibG9nLmNzZG4ubmV0L1JyaW5nb18=,size_16,color_FFFFFF,t_70" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-74哪些情况需要建索引" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#74哪些情况需要建索引"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>7.4.哪些情况需要建索引</h2>
<ul>
<li>主键自动建立主键索引（唯一 + 非空）。</li>
<li>频繁作为查询条件的字段应该创建索引。</li>
<li>查询中与其他表关联的字段，外键关系建立索引。</li>
<li>查询中排序的字段，排序字段若通过索引去访问将大大提高排序速度。</li>
<li>查询中统计或者分组字段（group by也和索引有关）。</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-75那些情况不要建索引" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#75那些情况不要建索引"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>7.5.那些情况不要建索引</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<p>记录太少的表。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>经常增删改的表。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>频繁更新的字段不适合创建索引。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Where条件里用不到的字段不创建索引。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>假如一个表有10万行记录，有一个字段A只有true和false两种值，并且每个值的分布概率大约为50%，那么对A字段建索引一般不会提高数据库的查询速度。索引的选择性是指索引列中不同值的数目与表中记录数的比。如果一个表中有2000条记录，表索引列有1980个不同的值，那么这个索引的选择性就是1980/2000=0.99。一个索引的选择性越接近于1，这个索引的效率就越高。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1><a id="user-content-8性能分析" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#8性能分析"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>8.性能分析</h1>
<h2><a id="user-content-81explain简介" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#81explain简介"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>8.1.EXPLAIN简介</h2>
<blockquote>
<p>EXPLAIN是什么？</p>
</blockquote>
<p>EXPLAIN：SQL的执行计划，使用EXPLAIN关键字可以模拟优化器执行SQL查询语句，从而知道MySQL是如何处理SQL语句的。</p>
<blockquote>
<p>EXPLAIN怎么使用？</p>
</blockquote>
<p>语法：<code>explain</code> + <code>SQL</code>。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> explain <span class="pl-k">select</span> <span class="pl-smi">*</span> from pms_category <span class="pl-cce">\G</span><span class="pl-k">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">***************************</span> 1. row <span class="pl-k">***************************</span>
           id: 1
  select_type: SIMPLE
        table: pms_category
   partitions: NULL
         type: ALL
possible_keys: NULL
          key: NULL
      key_len: NULL
          ref: NULL
         rows: 1425
     filtered: 100.00
        Extra: NULL
1 row <span class="pl-k">in</span> set, 1 warning (0.00 sec)</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>EXPLAIN能干嘛？</p>
</blockquote>
<p>可以查看以下信息：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>id</code>：表的读取顺序。</li>
<li><code>select_type</code>：数据读取操作的操作类型。</li>
<li><code>possible_keys</code>：哪些索引可以使用。</li>
<li><code>key</code>：哪些索引被实际使用。</li>
<li><code>ref</code>：表之间的引用。</li>
<li><code>rows</code>：每张表有多少行被优化器查询。</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-82explain字段" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#82explain字段"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>8.2.EXPLAIN字段</h2>
<blockquote>
<p>id</p>
</blockquote>
<p><code>id</code>：表的读取和加载顺序。</p>
<p>值有以下三种情况：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>id</code>相同，执行顺序由上至下。</li>
<li><code>id</code>不同，如果是子查询，id的序号会递增，<strong>id值越大优先级越高，越先被执行。</strong></li>
<li><code>id</code>相同不同，同时存在。<strong>永远是id大的优先级最高，id相等的时候顺序执行。</strong></li>
</ul>
<blockquote>
<p>select_type</p>
</blockquote>
<p><code>select_type</code>：数据查询的类型，主要是用于区别，普通查询、联合查询、子查询等的复杂查询。</p>
<ul>
<li><code>SIMPLE</code>：简单的<code>SELECT</code>查询，查询中不包含子查询或者<code>UNION </code>。</li>
<li><code>PRIMARY</code>：查询中如果包含任何复杂的子部分，最外层查询则被标记为<code>PRIMARY</code>。</li>
<li><code>SUBQUERY</code>：在<code>SELECT</code>或者<code>WHERE</code>子句中包含了子查询。</li>
<li><code>DERIVED</code>：在<code>FROM</code>子句中包含的子查询被标记为<code>DERIVED(衍生)</code>，MySQL会递归执行这些子查询，把结果放在临时表中。</li>
<li><code>UNION</code>：如果第二个<code>SELECT</code>出现在<code>UNION</code>之后，则被标记为<code>UNION</code>；若<code>UNION</code>包含在<code>FROM</code>子句的子查询中，外层<code>SELECT</code>将被标记为<code>DERIVED</code>。</li>
<li><code>UNION RESULT</code>：从<code>UNION</code>表获取结果的<code>SELECT</code>。</li>
</ul>
<blockquote>
<p>type</p>
</blockquote>
<p><code>type</code>：访问类型排列。</p>
<p><strong>从最好到最差依次是：</strong><code>system</code>&gt;<code>const</code>&gt;<code>eq_ref</code>&gt;<code>ref</code>&gt;<code>range</code>&gt;<code>index</code>&gt;<code>ALL</code>。除了<code>ALL</code>没有用到索引，其他级别都用到索引了。</p>
<p>一般来说，得保证查询至少达到<code>range</code>级别，最好达到<code>ref</code>。</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><code>system</code>：表只有一行记录（等于系统表），这是<code>const</code>类型的特例，平时不会出现，这个也可以忽略不计。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>const</code>：表示通过索引一次就找到了，<code>const</code>用于比较<code>primary key</code>或者<code>unique</code>索引。因为只匹配一行数据，所以很快。如将主键置于<code>where</code>列表中，MySQL就能将该查询转化为一个常量。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>eq_ref</code>：唯一性索引扫描，读取本表中和关联表表中的每行组合成的一行，查出来只有一条记录。除 了 <code>system</code> 和<code> const</code> 类型之外, 这是最好的联接类型。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>ref</code>：非唯一性索引扫描，返回本表和关联表某个值匹配的所有行，查出来有多条记录。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>range</code>：只检索给定范围的行，一般就是在<code>WHERE</code>语句中出现了<code>BETWEEN</code>、<code>&lt; &gt;</code>、<code>in</code>等的查询。这种范围扫描索引比全表扫描要好，因为它只需要开始于索引树的某一点，而结束于另一点，不用扫描全部索引。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>index</code>：<code>Full Index Scan</code>，全索引扫描，<code>index</code>和<code>ALL</code>的区别为<code>index</code>类型只遍历索引树。<strong>也就是说虽然<code>ALL</code>和<code>index</code>都是读全表，但是<code>index</code>是从索引中读的，<code>ALL</code>是从磁盘中读取的。</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>ALL</code>：<code>Full Table Scan</code>，没有用到索引，全表扫描。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<blockquote>
<p>possible_keys 和 key</p>
</blockquote>
<p><code>possible_keys</code>：显示可能应用在这张表中的索引，一个或者多个。查询涉及到的字段上若存在索引，则该索引将被列出，<strong>但不一定被查询实际使用。</strong></p>
<p><code>key</code>：实际使用的索引。如果为<code>NULL</code>，则没有使用索引。查询中如果使用了覆盖索引，则该索引仅仅出现在<code>key</code>列表中。</p>
<blockquote>
<p>key_len</p>
</blockquote>
<p><code>key_len</code>：表示索引中使用的字节数，可通过该列计算查询中使用的索引的长度。<code>key_len</code>显示的值为索引字段的最大可能长度，并非实际使用长度，即<code>key_len</code>是根据表定义计算而得，不是通过表内检索出的。在不损失精度的情况下，长度越短越好。</p>
<p><code>key_len</code>计算规则：<strong><a href="https://blog.csdn.net/qq_34930488/article/details/102931490" rel="nofollow">https://blog.csdn.net/qq_34930488/article/details/102931490</a></strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> desc pms_category<span class="pl-k">;</span>
+---------------+------------+------+-----+---------+----------------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Field         <span class="pl-k">|</span> Type       <span class="pl-k">|</span> Null <span class="pl-k">|</span> Key <span class="pl-k">|</span> Default <span class="pl-k">|</span> Extra          <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+---------------+------------+------+-----+---------+----------------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> cat_id        <span class="pl-k">|</span> bigint(20) <span class="pl-k">|</span> NO   <span class="pl-k">|</span> PRI <span class="pl-k">|</span> NULL    <span class="pl-k">|</span> auto_increment <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> name          <span class="pl-k">|</span> char(50)   <span class="pl-k">|</span> YES  <span class="pl-k">|</span>     <span class="pl-k">|</span> NULL    <span class="pl-k">|</span>                <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> parent_cid    <span class="pl-k">|</span> bigint(20) <span class="pl-k">|</span> YES  <span class="pl-k">|</span>     <span class="pl-k">|</span> NULL    <span class="pl-k">|</span>                <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> cat_level     <span class="pl-k">|</span> int(11)    <span class="pl-k">|</span> YES  <span class="pl-k">|</span>     <span class="pl-k">|</span> NULL    <span class="pl-k">|</span>                <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> show_status   <span class="pl-k">|</span> tinyint(4) <span class="pl-k">|</span> YES  <span class="pl-k">|</span>     <span class="pl-k">|</span> NULL    <span class="pl-k">|</span>                <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> sort          <span class="pl-k">|</span> int(11)    <span class="pl-k">|</span> YES  <span class="pl-k">|</span>     <span class="pl-k">|</span> NULL    <span class="pl-k">|</span>                <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> icon          <span class="pl-k">|</span> char(255)  <span class="pl-k">|</span> YES  <span class="pl-k">|</span>     <span class="pl-k">|</span> NULL    <span class="pl-k">|</span>                <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> product_unit  <span class="pl-k">|</span> char(50)   <span class="pl-k">|</span> YES  <span class="pl-k">|</span>     <span class="pl-k">|</span> NULL    <span class="pl-k">|</span>                <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> product_count <span class="pl-k">|</span> int(11)    <span class="pl-k">|</span> YES  <span class="pl-k">|</span>     <span class="pl-k">|</span> NULL    <span class="pl-k">|</span>                <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+---------------+------------+------+-----+---------+----------------+
9 rows <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-c1">set</span> (0.00 sec)


mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> explain <span class="pl-k">select</span> <span class="pl-smi">cat_id</span> from pms_category where cat_id between 10 and 20 <span class="pl-cce">\G</span><span class="pl-k">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">***************************</span> 1. row <span class="pl-k">***************************</span>
           id: 1
  select_type: SIMPLE
        table: pms_category
   partitions: NULL
         type: range
possible_keys: PRIMARY
          key: PRIMARY  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 用到了主键索引，通过查看表结构知道，cat_id是bigint类型，占用8个字节</span>
      key_len: 8        <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 这里只用到了cat_id主键索引，所以长度就是8！</span>
          ref: NULL
         rows: 11
     filtered: 100.00
        Extra: Using where<span class="pl-k">;</span> Using index
1 row <span class="pl-k">in</span> set, 1 warning (0.00 sec)</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>ref</p>
</blockquote>
<p><code>ref</code>：显示索引的哪一列被使用了，如果可能的话，是一个常数。哪些列或常量被用于查找索引列上的值。</p>
<blockquote>
<p>rows</p>
</blockquote>
<p><code>rows</code>：根据表统计信息及索引选用情况，大致估算出找到所需的记录需要读取的行数。</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Extra</p>
</blockquote>
<p><code>Extra</code>：包含不适合在其他列中显示但十分重要的额外信息。</p>
<ul>
<li><code>Using filesort</code>：说明MySQL会对数据使用一个外部的索引排序，而不是按照表内的索引顺序进行读取。<strong>MySQL中无法利用索引完成的排序操作成为"文件内排序"。</strong></li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 排序没有使用索引</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> explain <span class="pl-k">select</span> <span class="pl-smi">name</span> from pms_category where name=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Tangs<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> order by cat_level <span class="pl-cce">\G</span>
<span class="pl-k">***************************</span> 1. row <span class="pl-k">***************************</span>
           id: 1
  select_type: SIMPLE
        table: pms_category
   partitions: NULL
         type: ref
possible_keys: idx_name_parentCid_catLevel
          key: idx_name_parentCid_catLevel
      key_len: 201
          ref: const
         rows: 1
     filtered: 100.00
        Extra: Using where<span class="pl-k">;</span> Using index<span class="pl-k">;</span> Using filesort
1 row <span class="pl-k">in</span> set, 1 warning (0.00 sec)

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 排序使用到了索引</span>

mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> explain <span class="pl-k">select</span> <span class="pl-smi">name</span> from pms_category where name=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Tangs<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> order by parent_cid,cat_level<span class="pl-cce">\G</span>
<span class="pl-k">***************************</span> 1. row <span class="pl-k">***************************</span>
           id: 1
  select_type: SIMPLE
        table: pms_category
   partitions: NULL
         type: ref
possible_keys: idx_name_parentCid_catLevel
          key: idx_name_parentCid_catLevel
      key_len: 201
          ref: const
         rows: 1
     filtered: 100.00
        Extra: Using where<span class="pl-k">;</span> Using index
1 row <span class="pl-k">in</span> set, 1 warning (0.00 sec)</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p><code>Using temporary</code>：使用了临时表保存中间结果，MySQL在対查询结果排序时使用了临时表。常见于排序<code>order by</code>和分组查询<code>group by</code>。<strong>临时表対系统性能损耗很大。</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>Using index</code>：表示相应的<code>SELECT</code>操作中使用了覆盖索引，避免访问了表的数据行，效率不错！如果同时出现<code>Using where</code>，表示索引被用来执行索引键值的查找；如果没有同时出现<code>Using where</code>，表明索引用来读取数据而非执行查找动作。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 覆盖索引</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 就是select的数据列只用从索引中就能够取得，不必从数据表中读取，换句话说查询列要被所使用的索引覆盖。</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 注意：如果要使用覆盖索引，一定不能写SELECT *，要写出具体的字段。</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> explain <span class="pl-k">select</span> <span class="pl-smi">cat_id</span> from pms_category <span class="pl-cce">\G</span><span class="pl-k">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">***************************</span> 1. row <span class="pl-k">***************************</span>
           id: 1
  select_type: SIMPLE
        table: pms_category
   partitions: NULL
         type: index
possible_keys: NULL       
          key: PRIMARY
      key_len: 8
          ref: NULL
         rows: 1425
     filtered: 100.00
        Extra: Using index   <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> select的数据列只用从索引中就能够取得，不必从数据表中读取   </span>
1 row <span class="pl-k">in</span> set, 1 warning (0.00 sec)</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>Using where</code>：表明使用了<code>WHERE</code>过滤。</li>
<li><code>Using join buffer</code>：使用了连接缓存。</li>
<li><code>impossible where</code>：<code>WHERE</code>子句的值总是false，不能用来获取任何元组。</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> explain <span class="pl-k">select</span> <span class="pl-smi">name</span> from pms_category where name = <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>zs<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> and name = <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>ls<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span><span class="pl-cce">\G</span>
<span class="pl-k">***************************</span> 1. row <span class="pl-k">***************************</span>
           id: 1
  select_type: SIMPLE
        table: NULL
   partitions: NULL
         type: NULL
possible_keys: NULL
          key: NULL
      key_len: NULL
          ref: NULL
         rows: NULL
     filtered: NULL
        Extra: Impossible WHERE   <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 不可能字段同时查到两个名字</span>
1 row <span class="pl-k">in</span> set, 1 warning (0.00 sec)</pre></div>
<h1><a id="user-content-9索引分析" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#9索引分析"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>9.索引分析</h1>
<h2><a id="user-content-91单表索引分析" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#91单表索引分析"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>9.1.单表索引分析</h2>
<blockquote>
<p>数据准备</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-k">DROP</span> <span class="pl-k">TABLE</span> IF EXISTS <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>article<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>;

<span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">TABLE</span> <span class="pl-en">IF</span> NOT EXISTS <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>article<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">INT</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>) UNSIGNED <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> <span class="pl-k">PRIMARY KEY</span> AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>主键<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>author_id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">INT</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>) UNSIGNED <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>作者id<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>category_id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">INT</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>) UNSIGNED <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>分类id<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>views<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">INT</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>) UNSIGNED <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>被查看的次数<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>comments<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">INT</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>) UNSIGNED <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>回帖的备注<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>title<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">VARCHAR</span>(<span class="pl-c1">255</span>) <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>标题<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>content<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">VARCHAR</span>(<span class="pl-c1">255</span>) <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>正文内容<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
) COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>文章<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>article<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>author_id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>category_id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>views<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>comments<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>title<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>content<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>article<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>author_id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>category_id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>views<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>comments<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>title<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>content<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2</span>,<span class="pl-c1">2</span>,<span class="pl-c1">2</span>,<span class="pl-c1">2</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>2<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>2<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>article<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>author_id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>category_id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>views<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>comments<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>title<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>content<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-c1">3</span>,<span class="pl-c1">3</span>,<span class="pl-c1">3</span>,<span class="pl-c1">3</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>3<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>3<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>article<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>author_id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>category_id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>views<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>comments<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>title<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>content<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">3</span>,<span class="pl-c1">3</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>3<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>3<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>article<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>author_id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>category_id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>views<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>comments<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>title<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>content<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">4</span>,<span class="pl-c1">4</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>4<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>4<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>案例：查询<code>category_id</code>为1且<code>comments</code>大于1的情况下，<code>views</code>最多的<code>article_id</code>。</p>
</blockquote>
<p>1、编写SQL语句并查看SQL执行计划。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 1、sql语句</span>
SELECT id,author_id FROM article WHERE category_id = 1 AND comments <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> 1 ORDER BY views DESC LIMIT 1<span class="pl-k">;</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 2、sql执行计划</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> EXPLAIN SELECT id,author_id FROM article WHERE category_id = 1 AND comments <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> 1 ORDER BY views DESC LIMIT 1<span class="pl-cce">\G</span>
<span class="pl-k">***************************</span> 1. row <span class="pl-k">***************************</span>
           id: 1
  select_type: SIMPLE
        table: article
   partitions: NULL
         type: ALL
possible_keys: NULL
          key: NULL
      key_len: NULL
          ref: NULL
         rows: 5
     filtered: 20.00
        Extra: Using where<span class="pl-k">;</span> Using filesort  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 产生了文件内排序，需要优化SQL</span>
1 row <span class="pl-k">in</span> set, 1 warning (0.00 sec)</pre></div>
<p>2、创建索引<code>idx_article_ccv</code>。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">INDEX</span> <span class="pl-en">idx_article_ccv</span> <span class="pl-k">ON</span> article(category_id,comments,views);</pre></div>
<p>3、查看当前索引。</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/af1e0597f62f629e8ba87d79d6297371bdc277d81764759cf5b71c828d17ae32/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333133343135343136322e706e673f782d6f73732d70726f636573733d696d6167652f77617465726d61726b2c747970655f5a6d46755a33706f5a57356e6147567064476b2c736861646f775f31302c746578745f6148523063484d364c7939696247396e4c6d4e7a5a473475626d56304c314a796157356e6231383d2c73697a655f31362c636f6c6f725f4646464646462c745f3730"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/af1e0597f62f629e8ba87d79d6297371bdc277d81764759cf5b71c828d17ae32/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333133343135343136322e706e673f782d6f73732d70726f636573733d696d6167652f77617465726d61726b2c747970655f5a6d46755a33706f5a57356e6147567064476b2c736861646f775f31302c746578745f6148523063484d364c7939696247396e4c6d4e7a5a473475626d56304c314a796157356e6231383d2c73697a655f31362c636f6c6f725f4646464646462c745f3730" alt="show index" data-canonical-src="https://img-blog.csdnimg.cn/20200803134154162.png?x-oss-process=image/watermark,type_ZmFuZ3poZW5naGVpdGk,shadow_10,text_aHR0cHM6Ly9ibG9nLmNzZG4ubmV0L1JyaW5nb18=,size_16,color_FFFFFF,t_70" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p>4、查看现在SQL语句的执行计划。</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/56ce8afcc1cd7f087865200545bfa51bd816a8a17d7009ea16671b4d04816cf7/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333133343534393931342e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/56ce8afcc1cd7f087865200545bfa51bd816a8a17d7009ea16671b4d04816cf7/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333133343534393931342e706e67" alt="explain" data-canonical-src="https://img-blog.csdnimg.cn/20200803134549914.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p>我们发现，创建符合索引<code>idx_article_ccv</code>之后，虽然解决了全表扫描的问题，但是在<code>order by</code>排序的时候没有用到索引，MySQL居然还是用的<code>Using filesort</code>，为什么？</p>
<p>5、我们试试把SQL修改为<code>SELECT id,author_id FROM article WHERE category_id = 1 AND comments = 1 ORDER BY views DESC LIMIT 1;</code>看看SQL的执行计划。</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/28dd8243d541f134f8f809f075f1cd6874bb59572916e1ccacebcdcaaa12e5e6/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333133353232383934352e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/28dd8243d541f134f8f809f075f1cd6874bb59572916e1ccacebcdcaaa12e5e6/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333133353232383934352e706e67" alt="explain" data-canonical-src="https://img-blog.csdnimg.cn/20200803135228945.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p>推论：当<code>comments &gt; 1</code>的时候<code>order by</code>排序<code>views</code>字段索引就用不上，但是当<code>comments = 1</code>的时候<code>order by</code>排序<code>views</code>字段索引就可以用上！！！<strong>所以，范围之后的索引会失效。</strong></p>
<p>6、我们现在知道<strong>范围之后的索引会失效</strong>，原来的索引<code>idx_article_ccv</code>最后一个字段<code>views</code>会失效，那么我们如果删除这个索引，创建<code>idx_article_cv</code>索引呢？？？？</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 创建索引 idx_article_cv <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">INDEX</span> <span class="pl-en">idx_article_cv</span> <span class="pl-k">ON</span> article(category_id,views);</pre></div>
<p>查看当前的索引</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/03db6d5572b7c3bc6751f6ca23b1adf5b7a29114c8ef267eb5e9a1f69a08f64a/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333134303534323931322e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/03db6d5572b7c3bc6751f6ca23b1adf5b7a29114c8ef267eb5e9a1f69a08f64a/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333134303534323931322e706e67" alt="show index" data-canonical-src="https://img-blog.csdnimg.cn/20200803140542912.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p>7、当前索引是<code>idx_article_cv</code>，来看一下SQL执行计划。</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/b376f7631bc044d648ea335946db5ab23c8d1e1e2f21b838d4589df87bd31cee/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333134303935313830332e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/b376f7631bc044d648ea335946db5ab23c8d1e1e2f21b838d4589df87bd31cee/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333134303935313830332e706e67" alt="explain" data-canonical-src="https://img-blog.csdnimg.cn/20200803140951803.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-92两表索引分析" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#92两表索引分析"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>9.2.两表索引分析</h2>
<blockquote>
<p>数据准备</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-k">DROP</span> <span class="pl-k">TABLE</span> IF EXISTS <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>class<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>;
<span class="pl-k">DROP</span> <span class="pl-k">TABLE</span> IF EXISTS <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>book<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>;

<span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">TABLE</span> <span class="pl-en">IF</span> NOT EXISTS <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>class<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">INT</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>) UNSIGNED <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> <span class="pl-k">PRIMARY KEY</span> AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>主键<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>card<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">INT</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>) UNSIGNED <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>分类<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> 
) COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>商品类别<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">TABLE</span> <span class="pl-en">IF</span> NOT EXISTS <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>book<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>bookid<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">INT</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>) UNSIGNED <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> <span class="pl-k">PRIMARY KEY</span> AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>主键<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>card<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">INT</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>) UNSIGNED <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>分类<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
) COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>书籍<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>两表连接查询的SQL执行计划</p>
</blockquote>
<p>1、不创建索引的情况下，SQL的执行计划。</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/d685273f061f276a50830f79a10afdc652705dd91e09678185779c28d1054efa/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333134333535373138372e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/d685273f061f276a50830f79a10afdc652705dd91e09678185779c28d1054efa/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333134333535373138372e706e67" alt="explain" data-canonical-src="https://img-blog.csdnimg.cn/20200803143557187.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p><code>book</code>和<code>class</code>两张表都是没有使用索引，全表扫描，那么如果进行优化，索引是创建在<code>book</code>表还是创建在<code>class</code>表呢？下面进行大胆的尝试！</p>
<p>2、左表(<code>book</code>表)创建索引。</p>
<p>创建索引<code>idx_book_card</code></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 在book表创建索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">INDEX</span> <span class="pl-en">idx_book_card</span> <span class="pl-k">ON</span> book(card);</pre></div>
<p>在<code>book</code>表中有<code>idx_book_card</code>索引的情况下，查看SQL执行计划</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/98351261a6a2fc6afb3c2eff158568aed21b745ad15b1bb545ffb8ed838584b0/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333134343432393334392e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/98351261a6a2fc6afb3c2eff158568aed21b745ad15b1bb545ffb8ed838584b0/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333134343432393334392e706e67" alt="explain" data-canonical-src="https://img-blog.csdnimg.cn/20200803144429349.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p>3、删除<code>book</code>表的索引，右表(<code>class</code>表)创建索引。</p>
<p>创建索引<code>idx_class_card</code></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 在class表创建索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">INDEX</span> <span class="pl-en">idx_class_card</span> <span class="pl-k">ON</span> class(card);</pre></div>
<p>在<code>class</code>表中有<code>idx_class_card</code>索引的情况下，查看SQL执行计划</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/a4c2cf4a2f3745f7281fa5abeb0ceeb96c68da201d0899e55eeb0478710847fb/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333134353033303539372e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/a4c2cf4a2f3745f7281fa5abeb0ceeb96c68da201d0899e55eeb0478710847fb/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333134353033303539372e706e67" alt="explain" data-canonical-src="https://img-blog.csdnimg.cn/20200803145030597.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p><strong>由此可见，左连接将索引创建在右表上更合适，右连接将索引创建在左表上更合适。</strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-93三张表索引分析" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#93三张表索引分析"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>9.3.三张表索引分析</h2>
<blockquote>
<p>数据准备</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-k">DROP</span> <span class="pl-k">TABLE</span> IF EXISTS <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>phone<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>;

<span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">TABLE</span> <span class="pl-en">IF</span> NOT EXISTS <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>phone<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>phone_id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">INT</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>) UNSIGNED <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> <span class="pl-k">PRIMARY KEY</span> AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>主键<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>card<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">INT</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>) UNSIGNED <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>分类<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> 
) COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>手机<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>三表连接查询SQL优化</p>
</blockquote>
<p>1、不加任何索引，查看SQL执行计划。</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/9dcd7591ba18a63cc467bb82a603bbcb1a89793f61de5de0710a6126b54bf380/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333136303633313738362e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/9dcd7591ba18a63cc467bb82a603bbcb1a89793f61de5de0710a6126b54bf380/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333136303633313738362e706e67" alt="explain" data-canonical-src="https://img-blog.csdnimg.cn/20200803160631786.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p>2、根据两表查询优化的经验，左连接需要在右表上添加索引，所以尝试在<code>book</code>表和<code>phone</code>表上添加索引。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 在book表创建索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">INDEX</span> <span class="pl-en">idx_book_card</span> <span class="pl-k">ON</span> book(card);

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 在phone表上创建索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">INDEX</span> <span class="pl-en">idx_phone_card</span> <span class="pl-k">ON</span> phone(card);</pre></div>
<p>再次执行SQL的执行计划</p>
