<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/f9108f20d0c1b7412e1b6158bd50761dbbd264453aa7ac3e0af28189f6ffe18f/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333136313031333838302e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/f9108f20d0c1b7412e1b6158bd50761dbbd264453aa7ac3e0af28189f6ffe18f/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333136313031333838302e706e67" alt="explain" data-canonical-src="https://img-blog.csdnimg.cn/20200803161013880.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-94结论" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#94结论"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>9.4.结论</h2>
<p><code>JOIN</code>语句的优化：</p>
<ul>
<li>尽可能减少<code>JOIN</code>语句中的<code>NestedLoop</code>（嵌套循环）的总次数：<strong>永远都是小的结果集驱动大的结果集</strong>。</li>
<li>优先优化<code>NestedLoop</code>的内层循环。</li>
<li>保证<code>JOIN</code>语句中被驱动表上<code>JOIN</code>条件字段已经被索引。</li>
<li>当无法保证被驱动表的<code>JOIN</code>条件字段被索引且内存资源充足的前提下，不要太吝惜<code>Join Buffer</code> 的设置。</li>
</ul>
<h1><a id="user-content-10索引失效" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#10索引失效"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>10.索引失效</h1>
<blockquote>
<p>数据准备</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">TABLE</span> `<span class="pl-en">staffs</span>`(
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">INT</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>) <span class="pl-k">PRIMARY KEY</span> AUTO_INCREMENT,
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">VARCHAR</span>(<span class="pl-c1">24</span>) <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> DEFAULT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span><span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>姓名<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">INT</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>) <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> DEFAULT <span class="pl-c1">0</span> COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>年龄<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>pos<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">VARCHAR</span>(<span class="pl-c1">20</span>) <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> DEFAULT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span><span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>职位<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>add_time<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">TIMESTAMP</span> <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> DEFAULT <span class="pl-c1">CURRENT_TIMESTAMP</span> COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>入职时间<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
)COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>员工记录表<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>pos<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Ringo<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">18</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>manager<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>pos<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>张三<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">20</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>dev<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>pos<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>李四<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">21</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>dev<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 创建索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">INDEX</span> <span class="pl-en">idx_staffs_name_age_pos</span> <span class="pl-k">ON</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>pos<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>);</pre></div>
<h2><a id="user-content-101索引失效的情况" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#101索引失效的情况"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>10.1.索引失效的情况</h2>
<ul>
<li>全值匹配我最爱。</li>
<li>最佳左前缀法则。</li>
<li>不在索引列上做任何操作（计算、函数、(自动or手动)类型转换），会导致索引失效而转向全表扫描。</li>
<li>索引中范围条件右边的字段会全部失效。</li>
<li>尽量使用覆盖索引（只访问索引的查询，索引列和查询列一致），减少<code>SELECT *</code>。</li>
<li>MySQL在使用<code>!=</code>或者<code>&lt;&gt;</code>的时候无法使用索引会导致全表扫描。</li>
<li><code>is null</code>、<code>is not null</code>也无法使用索引。</li>
<li><code>like</code>以通配符开头<code>%abc</code>索引失效会变成全表扫描。</li>
<li>字符串不加单引号索引失效。</li>
<li>少用<code>or</code>，用它来连接时会索引失效。</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-102最佳左前缀法则" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#102最佳左前缀法则"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>10.2.最佳左前缀法则</h2>
<blockquote>
<p>案例</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 用到了idx_staffs_name_age_pos索引中的name字段 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Ringo<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 用到了idx_staffs_name_age_pos索引中的name, age字段 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Ringo<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">18</span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 用到了idx_staffs_name_age_pos索引中的name，age，pos字段 这是属于全值匹配的情况！！！<span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Ringo<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">18</span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>pos<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>manager<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 索引没用上，ALL全表扫描 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">18</span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>pos<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>manager<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 索引没用上，ALL全表扫描 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>pos<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>manager<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 用到了idx_staffs_name_age_pos索引中的name字段，pos字段索引失效 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Ringo<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>pos<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>manager<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>概念</p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong>最佳左前缀法则：如果索引是多字段的复合索引，要遵守最佳左前缀法则。指的是查询从索引的最左前列开始并且不跳过索引中的字段。</strong></p>
<p><strong>口诀：带头大哥不能死，中间兄弟不能断。</strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-103索引列上不计算" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#103索引列上不计算"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>10.3.索引列上不计算</h2>
<blockquote>
<p>案例</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 现在要查询`name` = 'Ringo'的记录下面有两种方式来查询！</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 1、直接使用 字段 = 值的方式来计算</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SELECT <span class="pl-k">*</span> FROM <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> WHERE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> = <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Ringo<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span>
+----+-------+-----+---------+---------------------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> id <span class="pl-k">|</span> name  <span class="pl-k">|</span> age <span class="pl-k">|</span> pos     <span class="pl-k">|</span> add_time            <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+----+-------+-----+---------+---------------------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span>  1 <span class="pl-k">|</span> Ringo <span class="pl-k">|</span>  18 <span class="pl-k">|</span> manager <span class="pl-k">|</span> 2020-08-03 08:30:39 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+----+-------+-----+---------+---------------------+
1 row <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-c1">set</span> (0.00 sec)

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 2、使用MySQL内置的函数</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SELECT <span class="pl-k">*</span> FROM <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> WHERE LEFT(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, 5) = <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Ringo<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span>
+----+-------+-----+---------+---------------------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> id <span class="pl-k">|</span> name  <span class="pl-k">|</span> age <span class="pl-k">|</span> pos     <span class="pl-k">|</span> add_time            <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+----+-------+-----+---------+---------------------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span>  1 <span class="pl-k">|</span> Ringo <span class="pl-k">|</span>  18 <span class="pl-k">|</span> manager <span class="pl-k">|</span> 2020-08-03 08:30:39 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+----+-------+-----+---------+---------------------+
1 row <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-c1">set</span> (0.00 sec)</pre></div>
<p>我们发现以上两条SQL的执行结果都是一样的，但是执行效率有没有差距呢？？？</p>
<p>通过分析两条SQL的执行计划来分析性能。</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/2a12e082bbf1aaae5b35661d3775ccea89f5adb15836f466954e828b73d76f50/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333137313835373332352e706e673f782d6f73732d70726f636573733d696d6167652f77617465726d61726b2c747970655f5a6d46755a33706f5a57356e6147567064476b2c736861646f775f31302c746578745f6148523063484d364c7939696247396e4c6d4e7a5a473475626d56304c314a796157356e6231383d2c73697a655f31362c636f6c6f725f4646464646462c745f3730"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/2a12e082bbf1aaae5b35661d3775ccea89f5adb15836f466954e828b73d76f50/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333137313835373332352e706e673f782d6f73732d70726f636573733d696d6167652f77617465726d61726b2c747970655f5a6d46755a33706f5a57356e6147567064476b2c736861646f775f31302c746578745f6148523063484d364c7939696247396e4c6d4e7a5a473475626d56304c314a796157356e6231383d2c73697a655f31362c636f6c6f725f4646464646462c745f3730" alt="explain" data-canonical-src="https://img-blog.csdnimg.cn/20200803171857325.png?x-oss-process=image/watermark,type_ZmFuZ3poZW5naGVpdGk,shadow_10,text_aHR0cHM6Ly9ibG9nLmNzZG4ubmV0L1JyaW5nb18=,size_16,color_FFFFFF,t_70" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p><strong>由此可见，在索引列上进行计算，会使索引失效。</strong></p>
<p><strong>口诀：索引列上不计算。</strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-104范围之后全失效" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#104范围之后全失效"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>10.4.范围之后全失效</h2>
<blockquote>
<p>案例</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 用到了idx_staffs_name_age_pos索引中的name，age，pos字段 这是属于全值匹配的情况！！！<span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Ringo<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">18</span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>pos<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>manager<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;


<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 用到了idx_staffs_name_age_pos索引中的name，age字段，pos字段索引失效 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>张三<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">18</span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>pos<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>dev<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;</pre></div>
<p>查看上述SQL的执行计划</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/d5fc8f73d516cc7f81d3761ba30dd267a072a74d99828fba54b6803f44168f85/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333137333335373738372e706e673f782d6f73732d70726f636573733d696d6167652f77617465726d61726b2c747970655f5a6d46755a33706f5a57356e6147567064476b2c736861646f775f31302c746578745f6148523063484d364c7939696247396e4c6d4e7a5a473475626d56304c314a796157356e6231383d2c73697a655f31362c636f6c6f725f4646464646462c745f3730"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/d5fc8f73d516cc7f81d3761ba30dd267a072a74d99828fba54b6803f44168f85/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333137333335373738372e706e673f782d6f73732d70726f636573733d696d6167652f77617465726d61726b2c747970655f5a6d46755a33706f5a57356e6147567064476b2c736861646f775f31302c746578745f6148523063484d364c7939696247396e4c6d4e7a5a473475626d56304c314a796157356e6231383d2c73697a655f31362c636f6c6f725f4646464646462c745f3730" alt="explain" data-canonical-src="https://img-blog.csdnimg.cn/20200803173357787.png?x-oss-process=image/watermark,type_ZmFuZ3poZW5naGVpdGk,shadow_10,text_aHR0cHM6Ly9ibG9nLmNzZG4ubmV0L1JyaW5nb18=,size_16,color_FFFFFF,t_70" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p><strong>由此可知，查询范围的字段使用到了索引，但是范围之后的索引字段会失效。</strong></p>
<p><strong>口诀：范围之后全失效。</strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-105覆盖索引尽量用" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#105覆盖索引尽量用"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>10.5.覆盖索引尽量用</h2>
<p>在写SQL的不要使用<code>SELECT *</code>，用什么字段就查询什么字段。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 没有用到覆盖索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Ringo<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">18</span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>pos<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>manager<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 用到了覆盖索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>pos<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Ringo<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">18</span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>pos<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>manager<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;</pre></div>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/71e1cea390c667b0696d9fcf15f58157d329f19e4dfdffa878efe20e695c8937/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333231333033313839332e706e673f782d6f73732d70726f636573733d696d6167652f77617465726d61726b2c747970655f5a6d46755a33706f5a57356e6147567064476b2c736861646f775f31302c746578745f6148523063484d364c7939696247396e4c6d4e7a5a473475626d56304c314a796157356e6231383d2c73697a655f31362c636f6c6f725f4646464646462c745f3730"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/71e1cea390c667b0696d9fcf15f58157d329f19e4dfdffa878efe20e695c8937/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333231333033313839332e706e673f782d6f73732d70726f636573733d696d6167652f77617465726d61726b2c747970655f5a6d46755a33706f5a57356e6147567064476b2c736861646f775f31302c746578745f6148523063484d364c7939696247396e4c6d4e7a5a473475626d56304c314a796157356e6231383d2c73697a655f31362c636f6c6f725f4646464646462c745f3730" alt="使用覆盖索引" data-canonical-src="https://img-blog.csdnimg.cn/20200803213031893.png?x-oss-process=image/watermark,type_ZmFuZ3poZW5naGVpdGk,shadow_10,text_aHR0cHM6Ly9ibG9nLmNzZG4ubmV0L1JyaW5nb18=,size_16,color_FFFFFF,t_70" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p><strong>口诀：查询一定不用<code>*</code></strong>。</p>
<h2><a id="user-content-106不等有时会失效" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#106不等有时会失效"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>10.6.不等有时会失效</h2>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 会使用到覆盖索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>pos<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">!=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Ringo<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 索引失效 全表扫描 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">!=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Ringo<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;</pre></div>
<h2><a id="user-content-107like百分加右边" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#107like百分加右边"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>10.7.like百分加右边</h2>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 索引失效 全表扫描 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">LIKE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>%ing%<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 索引失效 全表扫描 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">LIKE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>%ing<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 使用索引范围查询 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">LIKE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Rin%<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;</pre></div>
<p><strong>口诀：<code>like</code>百分加右边。</strong></p>
<p>如果一定要使用<code>%like</code>，而且还要保证索引不失效，那么使用覆盖索引来编写SQL。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 使用到了覆盖索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">LIKE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>%in%<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 使用到了覆盖索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">LIKE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>%in%<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 使用到了覆盖索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">LIKE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>%in%<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 使用到了覆盖索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>pos<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">LIKE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>%in%<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 使用到了覆盖索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">LIKE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>%in%<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 使用到了覆盖索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">LIKE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>%in%<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 使用到了覆盖索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>pos<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">LIKE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>%in<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 使用到了覆盖索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>pos<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">LIKE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>%na<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 索引失效 全表扫描 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>pos<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>add_time<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">LIKE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>%in<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;</pre></div>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/0df8d1d9c08e5529c7f30f90b36f75054d695e91e0cf36f5c479a4edb2053cce/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333232303734333230362e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/0df8d1d9c08e5529c7f30f90b36f75054d695e91e0cf36f5c479a4edb2053cce/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830333232303734333230362e706e67" alt="模糊查询百分号一定加前边" data-canonical-src="https://img-blog.csdnimg.cn/20200803220743206.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p><strong>口诀：覆盖索引保两边。</strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-108字符要加单引号" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#108字符要加单引号"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>10.8.字符要加单引号</h2>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 使用到了覆盖索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Ringo<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 使用到了覆盖索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">2000</span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 索引失效 全表扫描 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>staffs<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">2000</span>;</pre></div>
<p>这里name = 2000在MySQL中会发生强制类型转换，将数字转成字符串。</p>
<p><strong>口诀：字符要加单引号。</strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-109索引相关题目" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#109索引相关题目"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>10.9.索引相关题目</h2>
<p><strong>假设index(a,b,c)</strong></p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Where语句</th>
<th>索引是否被使用</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>where a = 3</td>
<td>Y，使用到a</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>where a = 3 and b = 5</td>
<td>Y，使用到a，b</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>where a = 3 and b = 5</td>
<td>Y，使用到a，b，c</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>where b = 3 或者 where b = 3 and c = 4 或者 where c = 4</td>
<td>N，没有用到a字段</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>where a = 3 and c = 5</td>
<td>使用到a，但是没有用到c，因为b断了</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>where a = 3 and b &gt; 4 and c = 5</td>
<td>使用到a，b，但是没有用到c，因为c在范围之后</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>where a = 3 and b like 'kk%' and c = 4</td>
<td>Y，a，b，c都用到</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>where a = 3 and b like '%kk' and c = 4</td>
<td>只用到a</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>where a = 3 and b like '%kk%' and c = 4</td>
<td>只用到a</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>where a = 3 and b like 'k%kk%' and c = 4</td>
<td>Y，a，b，c都用到</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h2><a id="user-content-1010面试题分析" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#1010面试题分析"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>10.10.面试题分析</h2>
<blockquote>
<p>数据准备</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 创建表 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">TABLE</span> `<span class="pl-en">test03</span>`(
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">INT</span> <span class="pl-k">PRIMARY KEY</span> <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> AUTO_INCREMENT,
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c1<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">CHAR</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>),
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c2<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">CHAR</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>),
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c3<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">CHAR</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>),
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c4<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">CHAR</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>),
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c5<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">CHAR</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>)
);

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 插入数据 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test03<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c1<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c2<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c3<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c4<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c5<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a2<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a3<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a4<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a5<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test03<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c1<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c2<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c3<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c4<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c5<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>b1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>b22<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>b3<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>b4<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>b5<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test03<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c1<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c2<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c3<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c4<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c5<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>c1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>c2<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>c3<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>c4<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>c5<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test03<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c1<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c2<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c3<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c4<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c5<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>d1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>d2<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>d3<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>d4<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>d5<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test03<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c1<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c2<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c3<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c4<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c5<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>e1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>e2<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>e3<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>e4<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>e5<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 创建复合索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">INDEX</span> <span class="pl-en">idx_test03_c1234</span> <span class="pl-k">ON</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test03<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c1<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c2<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c3<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c4<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>);</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>题目</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 最好索引怎么创建的，就怎么用，按照顺序使用，避免让MySQL再自己去翻译一次 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 1.全值匹配 用到索引c1 c2 c3 c4全字段 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test03<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c1<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c2<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a2<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c3<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a3<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c4<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a4<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 2.用到索引c1 c2 c3 c4全字段 MySQL的查询优化器会优化SQL语句的顺序<span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test03<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c1<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c2<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a2<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c4<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a4<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c3<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a3<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 3.用到索引c1 c2 c3 c4全字段 MySQL的查询优化器会优化SQL语句的顺序<span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test03<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c4<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a4<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c3<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a3<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c2<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a2<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c1<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 4.用到索引c1 c2 c3字段，c4字段失效，范围之后全失效 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test03<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c1<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c2<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a2<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c3<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a3<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c4<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a4<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 5.用到索引c1 c2 c3 c4全字段 MySQL的查询优化器会优化SQL语句的顺序<span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test03<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c1<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c2<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a2<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c4<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a4<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c3<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a3<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> </span>
<span class="pl-c">   6.用到了索引c1 c2 c3三个字段, c1和c2两个字段用于查找,  c3字段用于排序了但是没有统计到key_len中，c4字段失效</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test03<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c1<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c2<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a2<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c4<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a4<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c3<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 7.用到了索引c1 c2 c3三个字段，c1和c2两个字段用于查找, c3字段用于排序了但是没有统计到key_len中<span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test03<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c1<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c2<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a2<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c3<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> </span>
<span class="pl-c">   8.用到了索引c1 c2两个字段，c4失效，c1和c2两个字段用于查找，c4字段排序产生了Using filesort说明排序没有用到c4字段 </span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test03<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c1<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c2<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a2<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c4<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 9.用到了索引c1 c2 c3三个字段，c1用于查找，c2和c3用于排序 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test03<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c1<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c5<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a5<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c2<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c3<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 10.用到了c1一个字段，c1用于查找，c3和c2两个字段索引失效，产生了Using filesort <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test03<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c1<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c5<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a5<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c3<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c2<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 11.用到了c1 c2 c3三个字段，c1 c2用于查找，c2 c3用于排序 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test03<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c1<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span>  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c2<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a2<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> c2, c3;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 12.用到了c1 c2 c3三个字段，c1 c2用于查找，c2 c3用于排序 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test03<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c1<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span>  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c2<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a2<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c5<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a5<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> c2, c3;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> </span>
<span class="pl-c">   13.用到了c1 c2 c3三个字段，c1 c2用于查找，c2 c3用于排序 没有产生Using filesort </span>
<span class="pl-c">      因为之前c2这个字段已经确定了是'a2'了，这是一个常量，再去ORDER BY c3,c2 这时候c2已经不用排序了！</span>
<span class="pl-c">      所以没有产生Using filesort 和(10)进行对比学习！</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test03<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c1<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c2<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a2<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c5<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a5<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> c3, c2;



<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> GROUP BY 表面上是叫做分组，但是分组之前必定排序。 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 14.用到c1 c2 c3三个字段，c1用于查找，c2 c3用于排序，c4失效 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test03<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c1<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c4<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a4<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">GROUP BY</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c2<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c3<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 15.用到c1这一个字段，c4失效，c2和c3排序失效产生了Using filesort <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test03<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c1<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c4<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a4<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">GROUP BY</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c3<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>c2<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>;</pre></div>
<p><code>GROUP BY</code>基本上都需要进行排序，索引优化几乎和<code>ORDER BY</code>一致，但是<code>GROUP BY</code>会有临时表的产生。</p>
<h2><a id="user-content-1011总结" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#1011总结"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>10.11.总结</h2>
<p>索引优化的一般性建议：</p>
<ul>
<li>对于单值索引，尽量选择针对当前<code>query</code>过滤性更好的索引。</li>
<li>在选择复合索引的时候，当前<code>query</code>中过滤性最好的字段在索引字段顺序中，位置越靠前越好。</li>
<li>在选择复合索引的时候，尽量选择可以能够包含当前<code>query</code>中的<code>where</code>子句中更多字段的索引。</li>
<li>尽可能通过分析统计信息和调整<code>query</code>的写法来达到选择合适索引的目的。</li>
</ul>
<p>口诀：</p>
<ul>
<li>带头大哥不能死。</li>
<li>中间兄弟不能断。</li>
<li>索引列上不计算。</li>
<li>范围之后全失效。</li>
<li>覆盖索引尽量用。</li>
<li>不等有时会失效。</li>
<li>like百分加右边。</li>
<li>字符要加单引号。</li>
<li>一般SQL少用or。</li>
</ul>
<h1><a id="user-content-11分析慢sql的步骤" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#11分析慢sql的步骤"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>11.分析慢SQL的步骤</h1>
<p>分析：</p>
<p>1、观察，至少跑1天，看看生产的慢SQL情况。</p>
<p>2、开启慢查询日志，设置阈值，比如超过5秒钟的就是慢SQL，并将它抓取出来。</p>
<p>3、explain + 慢SQL分析。</p>
<p>4、show Profile。</p>
<p>5、运维经理 OR DBA，进行MySQL数据库服务器的参数调优。</p>
<p>总结（大纲）：</p>
<p>1、慢查询的开启并捕获。</p>
<p>2、explain + 慢SQL分析。</p>
<p>3、show Profile查询SQL在MySQL数据库中的执行细节和生命周期情况。</p>
<p>4、MySQL数据库服务器的参数调优。</p>
<h1><a id="user-content-12查询优化" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#12查询优化"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>12.查询优化</h1>
<h2><a id="user-content-121小表驱动大表" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#121小表驱动大表"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>12.1.小表驱动大表</h2>
<blockquote>
<p>优化原则：对于MySQL数据库而言，永远都是小表驱动大表。</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-java"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/**</span></span>
<span class="pl-c">* 举个例子：可以使用嵌套的for循环来理解小表驱动大表。</span>
<span class="pl-c">* 以下两个循环结果都是一样的，但是对于MySQL来说不一样，</span>
<span class="pl-c">* 第一种可以理解为，和MySQL建立5次连接每次查询1000次。</span>
<span class="pl-c">* 第一种可以理解为，和MySQL建立1000次连接每次查询5次。</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">for</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> i <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>; i <span class="pl-k">&lt;=</span> <span class="pl-c1">5</span>; i <span class="pl-k">++</span>){
    <span class="pl-k">for</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> j <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>; j <span class="pl-k">&lt;=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1000</span>; j<span class="pl-k">++</span>){
        
    }
}
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~</span>
<span class="pl-k">for</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> i <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>; i <span class="pl-k">&lt;=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1000</span>; i <span class="pl-k">++</span>){
    <span class="pl-k">for</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> j <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>; j <span class="pl-k">&lt;=</span> <span class="pl-c1">5</span>; j<span class="pl-k">++</span>){
        
    }
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>IN和EXISTS</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 优化原则：小表驱动大表，即小的数据集驱动大的数据集 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> IN适合B表比A表数据小的情况<span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>A<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">IN</span> (<span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>B<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>)

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> EXISTS适合B表比A表数据大的情况 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>A<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> EXISTS (<span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>B<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>B<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>.id <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>A<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>.id);</pre></div>
<p><strong>EXISTS：</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>语法：<code>SELECT....FROM tab WHERE EXISTS(subquery);</code>该语法可以理解为：</li>
<li>该语法可以理解为：将主查询的数据，放到子查询中做条件验证，根据验证结果（<code>true</code>或是<code>false</code>）来决定主查询的数据结果是否得以保留。</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>提示：</strong></p>
<ul>
<li><code>EXISTS(subquery)</code>子查询只返回<code>true</code>或者<code>false</code>，因此子查询中的<code>SELECT *</code>可以是<code>SELECT 1 OR SELECT X</code>，它们并没有区别。</li>
<li><code>EXISTS(subquery)</code>子查询的实际执行过程可能经过了优化而不是我们理解上的逐条对比，如果担心效率问题，可进行实际检验以确定是否有效率问题。</li>
<li><code>EXISTS(subquery)</code>子查询往往也可以用条件表达式，其他子查询或者<code>JOIN</code>替代，何种最优需要具体问题具体分析。</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-122order-by优化" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#122order-by优化"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>12.2.ORDER BY优化</h2>
<blockquote>
<p>数据准备</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">TABLE</span> `<span class="pl-en">talA</span>`(
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">INT</span>,
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>birth<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">TIMESTAMP</span> <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> DEFAULT <span class="pl-c1">CURRENT_TIMESTAMP</span>
);

<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>talA<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-c1">18</span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>talA<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-c1">19</span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>talA<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-c1">20</span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>talA<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-c1">21</span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>talA<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-c1">22</span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>talA<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-c1">23</span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>talA<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-c1">24</span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>talA<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-c1">25</span>);

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 创建索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">INDEX</span> <span class="pl-en">idx_talA_age_birth</span> <span class="pl-k">ON</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>talA<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>birth<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>);</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>案例</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 1.使用索引进行排序了 不会产生Using filesort <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>talA<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">20</span> <span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 2.使用索引进行排序了 不会产生Using filesort <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>talA<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">20</span> <span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>birth<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 3.没有使用索引进行排序 产生了Using filesort <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>talA<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">20</span> <span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>birth<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 4.没有使用索引进行排序 产生了Using filesort <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>talA<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">20</span> <span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>birth<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 5.没有使用索引进行排序 产生了Using filesort <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>talA<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>birth<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 6.没有使用索引进行排序 产生了Using filesort <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
