EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>talA<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>birth<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>2020-08-04 07:42:21<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>birth<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 7.使用索引进行排序了 不会产生Using filesort <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>talA<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>birth<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>2020-08-04 07:42:21<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 8.没有使用索引进行排序 产生了Using filesort <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
EXPLAIN <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>talA<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>age<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">ASC</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>birth<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">DESC</span>;</pre></div>
<p><code>ORDER BY</code>子句，尽量使用索引排序，避免使用<code>Using filesort</code>排序。</p>
<p>MySQL支持两种方式的排序，<code>FileSort</code>和<code>Index</code>，<code>Index</code>的效率高，它指MySQL扫描索引本身完成排序。<code>FileSort</code>方式效率较低。</p>
<p><code>ORDER BY</code>满足两情况，会使用<code>Index</code>方式排序：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>ORDER BY</code>语句使用索引最左前列。</li>
<li>使用<code>WHERE</code>子句与<code>ORDER BY</code>子句条件列组合满足索引最左前列。</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>结论：尽可能在索引列上完成排序操作，遵照索引建的最佳左前缀原则。</strong></p>
<blockquote>
<p>如果不在索引列上，File Sort有两种算法：MySQL就要启动双路排序算法和单路排序算法</p>
</blockquote>
<p>1、双路排序算法：MySQL4.1之前使用双路排序，字面意思就是两次扫描磁盘，最终得到数据，读取行指针和<code>ORDER BY</code>列，対他们进行排序，然后扫描已经排序好的列表，按照列表中的值重新从列表中读取对应的数据输出。<strong>一句话，从磁盘取排序字段，在<code>buffer</code>中进行排序，再从磁盘取其他字段。</strong></p>
<p>取一批数据，要对磁盘进行两次扫描，众所周知，IO是很耗时的，所以在MySQL4.1之后，出现了改进的算法，就是单路排序算法。</p>
<p>2、单路排序算法：从磁盘读取查询需要的所有列，按照<code>ORDER BY</code>列在<code>buffer</code>対它们进行排序，然后扫描排序后的列表进行输出，它的效率更快一些，避免了第二次读取数据。并且把随机IO变成了顺序IO，但是它会使用更多的空间，因为它把每一行都保存在内存中了。</p>
<p>由于单路排序算法是后出的，总体而言效率好过双路排序算法。</p>
<p>但是单路排序算法有问题：如果<code>SortBuffer</code>缓冲区太小，导致从磁盘中读取所有的列不能完全保存在<code>SortBuffer</code>缓冲区中，这时候单路复用算法就会出现问题，反而性能不如双路复用算法。</p>
<p><strong>单路复用算法的优化策略：</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>增大<code>sort_buffer_size</code>参数的设置。</li>
<li>增大<code>max_length_for_sort_data</code>参数的设置。</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>提高ORDER BY排序的速度：</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><code>ORDER BY</code>时使用<code>SELECT *</code>是大忌，查什么字段就写什么字段，这点非常重要。在这里的影响是：</p>
<ul>
<li>当查询的字段大小总和小于<code>max_length_for_sort_data</code>而且排序字段不是<code>TEXT|BLOB</code>类型时，会使用单路排序算法，否则使用多路排序算法。</li>
<li>两种排序算法的数据都有可能超出<code>sort_buffer</code>缓冲区的容量，超出之后，会创建<code>tmp</code>临时文件进行合并排序，导致多次IO，但是单路排序算法的风险会更大一些，所以要增大<code>sort_buffer_size</code>参数的设置。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>尝试提高<code>sort_buffer_size</code>：不管使用哪种算法，提高这个参数都会提高效率，当然，要根据系统的能力去提高，因为这个参数是针对每个进程的。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>尝试提高<code>max_length_for_sort_data</code>：提高这个参数，会增加用单路排序算法的概率。但是如果设置的太高，数据总容量<code>sort_buffer_size</code>的概率就增大，明显症状是高的磁盘IO活动和低的处理器使用率。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-123gorup-by优化" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#123gorup-by优化"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>12.3.GORUP BY优化</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<p><code>GROUP BY</code>实质是先排序后进行分组，遵照索引建的最佳左前缀。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>当无法使用索引列时，会使用<code>Using filesort</code>进行排序，增大<code>max_length_for_sort_data</code>参数的设置和增大<code>sort_buffer_size</code>参数的设置，会提高性能。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>WHERE</code>执行顺序高于<code>HAVING</code>，能写在<code>WHERE</code>限定条件里的就不要写在<code>HAVING</code>中了。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-124总结" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#124总结"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>12.4.总结</h2>
<p><strong>为排序使用索引</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>MySQL两种排序方式：<code>Using filesort</code>和<code>Index</code>扫描有序索引排序。</li>
<li>MySQL能为排序与查询使用相同的索引，创建的索引既可以用于排序也可以用于查询。</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 创建a b c三个字段的索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
idx_table_a_b_c(a, b, c)

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 1.ORDER BY 能使用索引最左前缀 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> a;
<span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> a, b;
<span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> a, b, c;
<span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> a <span class="pl-k">DESC</span>, b <span class="pl-k">DESC</span>, c <span class="pl-k">DESC</span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 2.如果WHERE子句中使用索引的最左前缀定义为常量，则ORDER BY能使用索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> a <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Ringo<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> b, c;
<span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> a <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Ringo<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> b <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Tangs<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> c;
<span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> a <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Ringo<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">AND</span> b <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">2000</span> <span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> b, c;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 3.不能使用索引进行排序 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> a <span class="pl-k">ASC</span>, b <span class="pl-k">DESC</span>, c <span class="pl-k">DESC</span>;  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 排序不一致 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> g <span class="pl-k">=</span> const <span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> b, c;   <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 丢失a字段索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> a <span class="pl-k">=</span> const <span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> c;      <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 丢失b字段索引 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> a <span class="pl-k">=</span> const <span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> a, d;   <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> d字段不是索引的一部分 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> a <span class="pl-k">IN</span> (...) <span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> b, c;  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 对于排序来说，多个相等条件(a=1 or a=2)也是范围查询 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span></pre></div>
<h1><a id="user-content-13慢查询日志" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#13慢查询日志"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>13.慢查询日志</h1>
<h2><a id="user-content-131基本介绍" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#131基本介绍"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>13.1.基本介绍</h2>
<blockquote>
<p>慢查询日志是什么？</p>
</blockquote>
<ul>
<li>MySQL的慢查询日志是MySQL提供的一种日志记录，它用来记录在MySQL中响应时间超过阈值的语句，具体指运行时间超过<code>long_query_time</code>值的SQL，则会被记录到慢查询日志中。</li>
<li><code>long_query_time</code>的默认值为10，意思是运行10秒以上的语句。</li>
<li>由慢查询日志来查看哪些SQL超出了我们的最大忍耐时间值，比如一条SQL执行超过5秒钟，我们就算慢SQL，希望能收集超过5秒钟的SQL，结合之前<code>explain</code>进行全面分析。</li>
</ul>
<blockquote>
<p>特别说明</p>
</blockquote>
<p>**默认情况下，MySQL数据库没有开启慢查询日志，**需要我们手动来设置这个参数。</p>
<p><strong>当然，如果不是调优需要的话，一般不建议启动该参数</strong>，因为开启慢查询日志会或多或少带来一定的性能影响。慢查询日志支持将日志记录写入文件。</p>
<blockquote>
<p>查看慢查询日志是否开以及如何开启</p>
</blockquote>
<ul>
<li>
<p>查看慢查询日志是否开启：<code>SHOW VARIABLES LIKE '%slow_query_log%';</code>。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>开启慢查询日志：<code>SET GLOBAL slow_query_log = 1;</code>。<strong>使用该方法开启MySQL的慢查询日志只对当前数据库生效，如果MySQL重启后会失效。</strong></p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 1、查看慢查询日志是否开启</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SHOW VARIABLES LIKE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>%slow_query_log%<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span>
+---------------------+--------------------------------------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Variable_name       <span class="pl-k">|</span> Value                                <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+---------------------+--------------------------------------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> slow_query_log      <span class="pl-k">|</span> OFF                                  <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> slow_query_log_file <span class="pl-k">|</span> /var/lib/mysql/1dcb5644392c-slow.log <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+---------------------+--------------------------------------+
2 rows <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-c1">set</span> (0.01 sec)

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 2、开启慢查询日志</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SET GLOBAL slow_query_log = 1<span class="pl-k">;</span>
Query OK, 0 rows affected (0.00 sec)</pre></div>
<p>如果要使慢查询日志永久开启，需要修改<code>my.cnf</code>文件，在<code>[mysqld]</code>下增加修改参数。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> my.cnf</span>
[mysqld]
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 1.这个是开启慢查询。注意ON需要大写</span>
slow_query_log=ON  

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 2.这个是存储慢查询的日志文件。这个文件不存在的话，需要自己创建</span>
slow_query_log_file=/var/lib/mysql/slow.log</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>开启了慢查询日志后，什么样的SQL才会被记录到慢查询日志里面呢？</p>
</blockquote>
<p>这个是由参数<code>long_query_time</code>控制的，默认情况下<code>long_query_time</code>的值为10秒。</p>
<p>MySQL中查看<code>long_query_time</code>的时间：<code>SHOW VARIABLES LIKE 'long_query_time%';</code>。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 查看long_query_time 默认是10秒</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 只有SQL的执行时间&gt;10才会被记录</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SHOW VARIABLES LIKE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>long_query_time%<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span>
+-----------------+-----------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Variable_name   <span class="pl-k">|</span> Value     <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+-----------------+-----------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> long_query_time <span class="pl-k">|</span> 10.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+-----------------+-----------+
1 row <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-c1">set</span> (0.00 sec)</pre></div>
<p>修改<code>long_query_time</code>的时间，需要在<code>my.cnf</code>修改配置文件</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>[mysqld]
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 这个是设置慢查询的时间，我设置的为1秒</span>
long_query_time=1</pre></div>
<p>查新慢查询日志的总记录条数：<code>SHOW GLOBAL STATUS LIKE '%Slow_queries%';</code>。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SHOW GLOBAL STATUS LIKE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>%Slow_queries%<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span>
+---------------+-------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Variable_name <span class="pl-k">|</span> Value <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+---------------+-------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Slow_queries  <span class="pl-k">|</span> 3     <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+---------------+-------+
1 row <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-c1">set</span> (0.00 sec)</pre></div>
<h2><a id="user-content-132日志分析工具" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#132日志分析工具"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>13.2.日志分析工具</h2>
<p>日志分析工具<code>mysqldumpslow</code>：在生产环境中，如果要手工分析日志，查找、分析SQL，显然是个体力活，MySQL提供了日志分析工具<code>mysqldumpslow</code>。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 1、mysqldumpslow --help 来查看mysqldumpslow的帮助信息</span>
root@1dcb5644392c:/usr/bin# mysqldumpslow --help
Usage: mysqldumpslow [ OPTS... ] [ LOGS... ]

Parse and summarize the MySQL slow query log. Options are

  --verbose    verbose
  --debug      debug
  --help       write this text to standard output

  -v           verbose
  -d           debug
  -s ORDER     what to sort by (al, at, ar, c, l, r, t), <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>at<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> is default  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 按照何种方式排序</span>
                al: average lock <span class="pl-k">time</span> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 平均锁定时间</span>
                ar: average rows sent <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 平均返回记录数</span>
                at: average query <span class="pl-k">time</span> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 平均查询时间</span>
                 c: count  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 访问次数</span>
                 l: lock <span class="pl-k">time</span>  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 锁定时间</span>
                 r: rows sent  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 返回记录</span>
                 t: query <span class="pl-k">time</span>  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 查询时间 </span>
  -r           reverse the sort order (largest last instead of first)
  -t NUM       just show the top n queries  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 返回前面多少条记录</span>
  -a           don<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>t abstract all numbers to N and strings to <span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>S<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">  -n NUM       abstract numbers with at least n digits within names</span>
<span class="pl-s">  -g PATTERN   grep: only consider stmts that include this string  </span>
<span class="pl-s">  -h HOSTNAME  hostname of db server for *-slow.log filename (can be wildcard),</span>
<span class="pl-s">               default is <span class="pl-pds">'</span></span><span class="pl-k">*</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>, i.e. match all</span>
<span class="pl-s">  -i NAME      name of server instance (if using mysql.server startup script)</span>
<span class="pl-s">  -l           don<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>t subtract lock <span class="pl-k">time</span> from total <span class="pl-k">time</span>
  
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 2、 案例</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 2.1、得到返回记录集最多的10个SQL</span>
mysqldumpslow -s r -t 10 /var/lib/mysql/slow.log
 
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 2.2、得到访问次数最多的10个SQL</span>
mysqldumpslow -s c -t 10 /var/lib/mysql/slow.log
 
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 2.3、得到按照时间排序的前10条里面含有左连接的查询语句</span>
mysqldumpslow -s t -t 10 -g <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>left join<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> /var/lib/mysql/slow.log

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 2.4、另外建议使用这些命令时结合|和more使用，否则出现爆屏的情况</span>
mysqldumpslow -s r -t 10 /var/lib/mysql/slow.log <span class="pl-k">|</span> more</pre></div>
<h1><a id="user-content-14批量插入数据脚本" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#14批量插入数据脚本"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>14.批量插入数据脚本</h1>
<h2><a id="user-content-141环境准备" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#141环境准备"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>14.1.环境准备</h2>
<blockquote>
<p>1、建表SQL。</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 1.dept表 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">TABLE</span> `<span class="pl-en">dept</span>` (
  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">int</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>) unsigned <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>主键<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>deptno<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">int</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>) unsigned <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> DEFAULT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>0<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>部门id<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>dname<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">varchar</span>(<span class="pl-c1">20</span>) <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> DEFAULT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span><span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>部门名字<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>loc<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">varchar</span>(<span class="pl-c1">13</span>) <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> DEFAULT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span><span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>部门地址<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-k">PRIMARY KEY</span> (<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>)
) ENGINE<span class="pl-k">=</span>InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET<span class="pl-k">=</span>utf8 COMMENT<span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>部门表<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> 2.emp表 <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">TABLE</span> `<span class="pl-en">emp</span>` (
  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">int</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>) unsigned <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>主键<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>empno<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">int</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>) unsigned <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> DEFAULT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>0<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>员工编号<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>ename<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">varchar</span>(<span class="pl-c1">20</span>) <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> DEFAULT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span><span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>员工名字<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>job<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">varchar</span>(<span class="pl-c1">9</span>) <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> DEFAULT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span><span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>职位<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>mgr<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">int</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>) unsigned <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> DEFAULT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>0<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>上级编号<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>hiredata<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">date</span> <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>入职时间<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>sal<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">decimal</span>(<span class="pl-c1">7</span>,<span class="pl-c1">2</span>) <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>薪水<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>comm<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">decimal</span>(<span class="pl-c1">7</span>,<span class="pl-c1">2</span>) <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>分红<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>deptno<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">int</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>) unsigned <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> DEFAULT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>0<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> COMMENT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>部门id<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-k">PRIMARY KEY</span> (<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>)
) ENGINE<span class="pl-k">=</span>InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET<span class="pl-k">=</span>utf8 COMMENT<span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>员工表<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>2、由于开启过慢查询日志，开启了<code>bin-log</code>，我们就必须为<code>function</code>指定一个参数，否则使用函数会报错。</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 在mysql中设置 </span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> log_bin_trust_function_creators 默认是关闭的 需要手动开启</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SHOW VARIABLES LIKE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>log_bin_trust_function_creators<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span>
+---------------------------------+-------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Variable_name                   <span class="pl-k">|</span> Value <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+---------------------------------+-------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> log_bin_trust_function_creators <span class="pl-k">|</span> OFF   <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+---------------------------------+-------+
1 row <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-c1">set</span> (0.00 sec)

mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SET GLOBAL log_bin_trust_function_creators=1<span class="pl-k">;</span>
Query OK, 0 rows affected (0.00 sec)</pre></div>
<p>上述修改方式MySQL重启后会失败，在<code>my.cnf</code>配置文件下修改永久有效。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>[mysqld]
log_bin_trust_function_creators=ON</pre></div>
<h2><a id="user-content-142创建函数" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#142创建函数"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>14.2.创建函数</h2>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 1、函数：随机产生字符串</span>
DELIMITER $$
<span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">FUNCTION</span> <span class="pl-en">rand_string</span>(n <span class="pl-k">INT</span>) RETURNS <span class="pl-k">VARCHAR</span>(<span class="pl-c1">255</span>)
<span class="pl-k">BEGIN</span>
    DECLARE chars_str <span class="pl-k">VARCHAR</span>(<span class="pl-c1">100</span>) DEFAULT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwsyzABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;
    DECLARE return_str <span class="pl-k">VARCHAR</span>(<span class="pl-c1">255</span>) DEFAULT <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span><span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;
    DECLARE i <span class="pl-k">INT</span> DEFAULT <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
    WHILE i <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span> n DO
    <span class="pl-k">SET</span> return_str <span class="pl-k">=</span> CONCAT(return_str,<span class="pl-c1">SUBSTRING</span>(chars_str,FLOOR(<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-k">+</span>RAND()<span class="pl-k">*</span><span class="pl-c1">52</span>),<span class="pl-c1">1</span>));
    <span class="pl-k">SET</span> i <span class="pl-k">=</span> i <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>;
    END WHILE;
    RETURN return_str;
END $$

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 2、函数：随机产生部门编号</span>
DELIMITER $$
<span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">FUNCTION</span> <span class="pl-en">rand_num</span>() RETURNS <span class="pl-k">INT</span>(<span class="pl-c1">5</span>)
<span class="pl-k">BEGIN</span>
    DECLARE i <span class="pl-k">INT</span> DEFAULT <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
    <span class="pl-k">SET</span> i <span class="pl-k">=</span> FLOOR(<span class="pl-c1">100</span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> RAND() <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-c1">10</span>);
    RETURN i;
END $$</pre></div>
<h2><a id="user-content-143创建存储过程" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#143创建存储过程"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>14.3.创建存储过程</h2>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 1、函数：向dept表批量插入</span>
DELIMITER $$
CREATE PROCEDURE insert_dept(<span class="pl-k">IN</span> START <span class="pl-k">INT</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>),<span class="pl-k">IN</span> max_num <span class="pl-k">INT</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>))
<span class="pl-k">BEGIN</span>
DECLARE i <span class="pl-k">INT</span> DEFAULT <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
    <span class="pl-k">SET</span> autocommit <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
    REPEAT
    <span class="pl-k">SET</span> i <span class="pl-k">=</span> i <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>;
    <span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> dept(deptno,dname,loc) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>((START <span class="pl-k">+</span> i),rand_string(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>),rand_string(<span class="pl-c1">8</span>));
    UNTIL i <span class="pl-k">=</span> max_num
    END REPEAT;
    <span class="pl-k">COMMIT</span>;
END $$

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 2、函数：向emp表批量插入</span>
DELIMITER $$
CREATE PROCEDURE insert_emp(<span class="pl-k">IN</span> START <span class="pl-k">INT</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>),<span class="pl-k">IN</span> max_num <span class="pl-k">INT</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>))
<span class="pl-k">BEGIN</span>
DECLARE i <span class="pl-k">INT</span> DEFAULT <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
    <span class="pl-k">SET</span> autocommit <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
    REPEAT
    <span class="pl-k">SET</span> i <span class="pl-k">=</span> i <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>;
    <span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> emp(empno,ename,job,mgr,hiredata,sal,comm,deptno) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>((START <span class="pl-k">+</span> i),rand_string(<span class="pl-c1">6</span>),<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>SALESMAN<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-c1">0001</span>,CURDATE(),<span class="pl-c1">2000</span>,<span class="pl-c1">400</span>,rand_num());
    UNTIL i <span class="pl-k">=</span> max_num
    END REPEAT;
    <span class="pl-k">COMMIT</span>;
END $$</pre></div>
<h2><a id="user-content-144调用存储过程" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#144调用存储过程"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>14.4.调用存储过程</h2>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 1、调用存储过程向dept表插入10个部门。</span>
DELIMITER ;
CALL insert_dept(<span class="pl-c1">100</span>,<span class="pl-c1">10</span>);

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 2、调用存储过程向emp表插入50万条数据。</span>
DELIMITER ;
CALL insert_emp(<span class="pl-c1">100001</span>,<span class="pl-c1">500000</span>);</pre></div>
<h1><a id="user-content-15show-profile" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#15show-profile"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>15.Show Profile</h1>
<blockquote>
<p>Show Profile是什么？</p>
</blockquote>
<p><code>Show Profile</code>：MySQL提供可以用来分析当前会话中语句执行的资源消耗情况。可以用于SQL的调优的测量。<strong>默认情况下，参数处于关闭状态，并保存最近15次的运行结果。</strong></p>
<blockquote>
<p>分析步骤</p>
</blockquote>
<p>1、是否支持，看看当前的MySQL版本是否支持。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 查看Show Profile功能是否开启</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SHOW VARIABLES LIKE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>profiling<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span>
+---------------+-------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Variable_name <span class="pl-k">|</span> Value <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+---------------+-------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> profiling     <span class="pl-k">|</span> OFF   <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+---------------+-------+
1 row <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-c1">set</span> (0.00 sec)</pre></div>
<p>2、开启<code>Show Profile</code>功能，默认是关闭的，使用前需要开启。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 开启Show Profile功能</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SET profiling=ON<span class="pl-k">;</span>
Query OK, 0 rows affected, 1 warning (0.00 sec)</pre></div>
<p>3、运行SQL</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>emp<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">GROUP BY</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>%<span class="pl-c1">10</span> <span class="pl-k">LIMIT</span> <span class="pl-c1">150000</span>;

<span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>emp<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">GROUP BY</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>%<span class="pl-c1">20</span> <span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> <span class="pl-c1">5</span>;</pre></div>
<p>4、查看结果，执行<code>SHOW PROFILES;</code></p>
<p><code>Duration</code>：持续时间。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SHOW PROFILES<span class="pl-k">;</span>
+----------+------------+---------------------------------------------------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Query_ID <span class="pl-k">|</span> Duration   <span class="pl-k">|</span> Query                                             <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+----------+------------+---------------------------------------------------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span>        1 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.00156100 <span class="pl-k">|</span> SHOW VARIABLES LIKE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>profiling<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>                   <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>        2 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.56296725 <span class="pl-k">|</span> SELECT <span class="pl-k">*</span> FROM <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>emp<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> GROUP BY <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>%10 LIMIT 150000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>        3 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.52105825 <span class="pl-k">|</span> SELECT <span class="pl-k">*</span> FROM <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>emp<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> GROUP BY <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>%10 LIMIT 150000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>        4 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.51279775 <span class="pl-k">|</span> SELECT <span class="pl-k">*</span> FROM <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>emp<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> GROUP BY <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>%20 ORDER BY 5   <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+----------+------------+---------------------------------------------------+
4 rows <span class="pl-k">in</span> set, 1 warning (0.00 sec)</pre></div>
<p>5、诊断SQL，<code>SHOW PROFILE cpu,block io FOR QUERY Query_ID;</code></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 这里的3是第四步中的Query_ID。</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 可以在SHOW PROFILE中看到一条SQL中完整的生命周期。</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SHOW PROFILE cpu,block io FOR QUERY 3<span class="pl-k">;</span>
+----------------------+----------+----------+------------+--------------+---------------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Status               <span class="pl-k">|</span> Duration <span class="pl-k">|</span> CPU_user <span class="pl-k">|</span> CPU_system <span class="pl-k">|</span> Block_ops_in <span class="pl-k">|</span> Block_ops_out <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+----------------------+----------+----------+------------+--------------+---------------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> starting             <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000097 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000090 <span class="pl-k">|</span>   0.000002 <span class="pl-k">|</span>            0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>             0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> checking permissions <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000010 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000009 <span class="pl-k">|</span>   0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>            0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>             0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Opening tables       <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000039 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000058 <span class="pl-k">|</span>   0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>            0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>             0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>

<span class="pl-k">|</span> System lock          <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000011 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>   0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>            0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>             0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> optimizing           <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000005 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>   0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>            0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>             0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> statistics           <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000023 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000037 <span class="pl-k">|</span>   0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>            0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>             0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
