<span class="pl-k">|</span> Creating tmp table   <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000041 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000053 <span class="pl-k">|</span>   0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>            0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>             0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Sorting result       <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000005 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>   0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>            0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>             0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> executing            <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000003 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>   0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>            0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>             0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Sending data         <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.520620 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.516267 <span class="pl-k">|</span>   0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>            0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>             0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Creating sort index  <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000060 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000051 <span class="pl-k">|</span>   0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>            0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>             0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> end                  <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000006 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>   0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>            0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>             0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> query end            <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000011 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>   0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>            0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>             0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> removing tmp table   <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000006 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>   0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>            0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>             0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> query end            <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000004 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>   0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>            0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>             0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> closing tables       <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000009 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>   0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>            0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>             0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> freeing items        <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000032 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000064 <span class="pl-k">|</span>   0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>            0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>             0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> cleaning up          <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000019 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>   0.000000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>            0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>             0 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+----------------------+----------+----------+------------+--------------+---------------+
20 rows <span class="pl-k">in</span> set, 1 warning (0.00 sec)</pre></div>
<p><code>Show Profile</code>查询参数备注：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>ALL</code>：显示所有的开销信息。</li>
<li><code>BLOCK IO</code>：显示块IO相关开销（通用）。</li>
<li><code>CONTEXT SWITCHES</code>：上下文切换相关开销。</li>
<li><code>CPU</code>：显示CPU相关开销信息（通用）。</li>
<li><code>IPC</code>：显示发送和接收相关开销信息。</li>
<li><code>MEMORY</code>：显示内存相关开销信息。</li>
<li><code>PAGE FAULTS</code>：显示页面错误相关开销信息。</li>
<li><code>SOURCE</code>：显示和Source_function。</li>
<li><code>SWAPS</code>：显示交换次数相关开销的信息。</li>
</ul>
<p>6、<code>Show Profile</code>查询列表，日常开发需要注意的结论：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>converting HEAP to MyISAM</code>：查询结果太大，内存都不够用了，往磁盘上搬了。</li>
<li><code>Creating tmp table</code>：创建临时表（拷贝数据到临时表，用完再删除），非常耗费数据库性能。</li>
<li><code>Copying to tmp table on disk</code>：把内存中的临时表复制到磁盘，危险！！！</li>
<li><code>locked</code>：死锁。</li>
</ul>
<h1><a id="user-content-16表锁偏读" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#16表锁偏读"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>16.表锁(偏读)</h1>
<p><strong>表锁特点：</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>表锁偏向<code>MyISAM</code>存储引擎，开销小，加锁快，无死锁，锁定粒度大，发生锁冲突的概率最高，并发度最低。</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-161环境准备" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#161环境准备"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>16.1.环境准备</h2>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 1、创建表</span>
<span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">TABLE</span> `<span class="pl-en">mylock</span>`(
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">INT</span> <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span> <span class="pl-k">PRIMARY KEY</span> AUTO_INCREMENT,
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">VARCHAR</span>(<span class="pl-c1">20</span>)
)ENGINE<span class="pl-k">=</span>MYISAM DEFAULT CHARSET<span class="pl-k">=</span>utf8 COMMENT<span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>测试表锁<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 2、插入数据</span>
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>mylock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>ZhangSan<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>mylock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>LiSi<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>mylock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>WangWu<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>mylock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>ZhaoLiu<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);</pre></div>
<h2><a id="user-content-162锁表的命令" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#162锁表的命令"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>16.2.锁表的命令</h2>
<blockquote>
<p>1、查看数据库表锁的命令。</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 查看数据库表锁的命令</span>
SHOW OPEN TABLES;</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>2、给<code>mylock</code>表上读锁，给<code>book</code>表上写锁。</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 给mylock表上读锁，给book表上写锁</span>
LOCK TABLE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>mylock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> READ, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>book<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> WRITE;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 查看当前表的状态</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SHOW OPEN TABLES;
<span class="pl-k">+</span><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span>------------------+------------------------------------------------------+--------+-------------+</span>
| Database           | Table                                                | In_use | Name_locked |
<span class="pl-k">+</span><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span>------------------+------------------------------------------------------+--------+-------------+</span>
| sql_analysis       | book                                                 |      <span class="pl-c1">1</span> |           <span class="pl-c1">0</span> |
| sql_analysis       | mylock                                               |      <span class="pl-c1">1</span> |           <span class="pl-c1">0</span> |
<span class="pl-k">+</span><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span>------------------+------------------------------------------------------+--------+-------------+</span></pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>3、释放表锁。</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 释放给表添加的锁</span>
UNLOCK TABLES;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 查看当前表的状态</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SHOW OPEN TABLES;
<span class="pl-k">+</span><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span>------------------+------------------------------------------------------+--------+-------------+</span>
| Database           | Table                                                | In_use | Name_locked |
<span class="pl-k">+</span><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span>------------------+------------------------------------------------------+--------+-------------+</span>
| sql_analysis       | book                                                 |      <span class="pl-c1">0</span> |           <span class="pl-c1">0</span> |
| sql_analysis       | mylock                                               |      <span class="pl-c1">0</span> |           <span class="pl-c1">0</span> |
<span class="pl-k">+</span><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span>------------------+------------------------------------------------------+--------+-------------+</span></pre></div>
<h2><a id="user-content-163读锁案例" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#163读锁案例"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>16.3.读锁案例</h2>
<blockquote>
<p>1、打开两个会话，<code>SESSION1</code>为<code>mylock</code>表添加读锁。</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 为mylock表添加读锁</span>
LOCK TABLE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>mylock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> READ;</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>2、打开两个会话，<code>SESSION1</code>是否可以读自己锁的表？是否可以修改自己锁的表？是否可以读其他的表？那么<code>SESSION2</code>呢？</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> SESSION1</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 问题1：SESSION1为mylock表加了读锁，可以读mylock表！</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SELECT <span class="pl-k">*</span> FROM <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>mylock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span>
+----+----------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> id <span class="pl-k">|</span> name     <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+----+----------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span>  1 <span class="pl-k">|</span> ZhangSan <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>  2 <span class="pl-k">|</span> LiSi     <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>  3 <span class="pl-k">|</span> WangWu   <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>  4 <span class="pl-k">|</span> ZhaoLiu  <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+----+----------+
4 rows <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-c1">set</span> (0.00 sec)

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 问题2：SESSION1为mylock表加了读锁，不可以修改mylock表！</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> UPDATE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>mylock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> SET <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> = <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>abc<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> WHERE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> = 1<span class="pl-k">;</span>
ERROR 1099 (HY000): Table <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>mylock<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> was locked with a READ lock and can<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>t be updated</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s"># 问题3：SESSION1为mylock表加了读锁，不可以读其他的表！</span>
<span class="pl-s">mysql&gt; SELECT * FROM `book`;</span>
<span class="pl-s">ERROR 1100 (HY000): Table <span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>book<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span> was not locked with LOCK TABLES</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s"># SESSION2</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s"># 问题1：SESSION1为mylock表加了读锁，SESSION2可以读mylock表！</span>
<span class="pl-s">mysql&gt; SELECT * FROM `mylock`;</span>
<span class="pl-s">+----+----------+</span>
<span class="pl-s">| id | name     |</span>
<span class="pl-s">+----+----------+</span>
<span class="pl-s">|  1 | ZhangSan |</span>
<span class="pl-s">|  2 | LiSi     |</span>
<span class="pl-s">|  3 | WangWu   |</span>
<span class="pl-s">|  4 | ZhaoLiu  |</span>
<span class="pl-s">+----+----------+</span>
<span class="pl-s">4 rows in set (0.00 sec)</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s"># 问题2：SESSION1为mylock表加了读锁，SESSION2修改mylock表会被阻塞，需要等待SESSION1释放mylock表！</span>
<span class="pl-s">mysql&gt; UPDATE `mylock` SET `name` = <span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>abc<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span> WHERE `id` = 1;</span>
<span class="pl-s">^C^C -- query aborted</span>
<span class="pl-s">ERROR 1317 (70100): Query execution was interrupted</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s"># 问题3：SESSION1为mylock表加了读锁，SESSION2可以读其他表！</span>
<span class="pl-s">mysql&gt; SELECT * FROM `book`;</span>
<span class="pl-s">+--------+------+</span>
<span class="pl-s">| bookid | card |</span>
<span class="pl-s">+--------+------+</span>
<span class="pl-s">|      1 |    1 |</span>
<span class="pl-s">|      7 |    4 |</span>
<span class="pl-s">|      8 |    4 |</span>
<span class="pl-s">|      9 |    5 |</span>
<span class="pl-s">|      5 |    6 |</span>
<span class="pl-s">|     17 |    6 |</span>
<span class="pl-s">|     15 |    8 |</span>
<span class="pl-s">+--------+------+</span>
<span class="pl-s">24 rows in set (0.00 sec)</span></pre></div>
<h2><a id="user-content-164写锁案例" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#164写锁案例"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>16.4.写锁案例</h2>
<blockquote>
<p>1、打开两个会话，<code>SESSION1</code>为<code>mylock</code>表添加写锁。</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 为mylock表添加写锁</span>
LOCK TABLE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>mylock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> WRITE;</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>2、打开两个会话，<code>SESSION1</code>是否可以读自己锁的表？是否可以修改自己锁的表？是否可以读其他的表？那么<code>SESSION2</code>呢？</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> SESSION1</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 问题1：SESSION1为mylock表加了写锁，可以读mylock的表！</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SELECT <span class="pl-k">*</span> FROM <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>mylock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span>
+----+----------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> id <span class="pl-k">|</span> name     <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+----+----------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span>  1 <span class="pl-k">|</span> ZhangSan <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>  2 <span class="pl-k">|</span> LiSi     <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>  3 <span class="pl-k">|</span> WangWu   <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>  4 <span class="pl-k">|</span> ZhaoLiu  <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+----+----------+
4 rows <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-c1">set</span> (0.00 sec)

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 问题2：SESSION1为mylock表加了写锁，可以修改mylock表!</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> UPDATE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>mylock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> SET <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> = <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>abc<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> WHERE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> = 1<span class="pl-k">;</span>
Query OK, 1 row affected (0.00 sec)
Rows matched: 1  Changed: 1  Warnings: 0

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 问题3：SESSION1为mylock表加了写锁，不能读其他表!</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SELECT <span class="pl-k">*</span> FROM <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>book<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span>
ERROR 1100 (HY000): Table <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>book<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> was not locked with LOCK TABLES

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> SESSION2</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 问题1：SESSION1为mylock表加了写锁，SESSION2读mylock表会阻塞，等待SESSION1释放！</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SELECT <span class="pl-k">*</span> FROM <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>mylock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span>
^C^C -- query aborted
ERROR 1317 (70100): Query execution was interrupted

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 问题2：SESSION1为mylock表加了写锁，SESSION2读mylock表会阻塞，等待SESSION1释放！</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> UPDATE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>mylock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> SET <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> = <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>abc<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> WHERE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> = 1<span class="pl-k">;</span>
^C^C -- query aborted
ERROR 1317 (70100): Query execution was interrupted

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 问题3：SESSION1为mylock表加了写锁，SESSION2可以读其他表！</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SELECT <span class="pl-k">*</span> FROM <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>book<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span>
+--------+------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> bookid <span class="pl-k">|</span> card <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+--------+------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span>      1 <span class="pl-k">|</span>    1 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>      7 <span class="pl-k">|</span>    4 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>      8 <span class="pl-k">|</span>    4 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>      9 <span class="pl-k">|</span>    5 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>      5 <span class="pl-k">|</span>    6 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>     17 <span class="pl-k">|</span>    6 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>     15 <span class="pl-k">|</span>    8 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+--------+------+
24 rows <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-c1">set</span> (0.00 sec)</pre></div>
<h2><a id="user-content-165案例结论" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#165案例结论"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>16.5.案例结论</h2>
<p><strong><code>MyISAM</code>引擎在执行查询语句<code>SELECT</code>之前，会自动给涉及到的所有表加读锁，在执行增删改之前，会自动给涉及的表加写锁。</strong></p>
<p>MySQL的表级锁有两种模式：</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>表共享读锁（Table Read Lock）。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>表独占写锁（Table Write Lock）。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>対<code>MyISAM</code>表进行操作，会有以下情况：</p>
<ul>
<li>対<code>MyISAM</code>表的读操作（加读锁），不会阻塞其他线程対同一表的读操作，但是会阻塞其他线程対同一表的写操作。只有当读锁释放之后，才会执行其他线程的写操作。</li>
<li>対<code>MyISAM</code>表的写操作（加写锁），会阻塞其他线程対同一表的读和写操作，只有当写锁释放之后，才会执行其他线程的读写操作。</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-166表锁分析" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#166表锁分析"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>16.6.表锁分析</h2>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SHOW STATUS LIKE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>table%<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span>
+----------------------------+-------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Variable_name              <span class="pl-k">|</span> Value <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+----------------------------+-------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Table_locks_immediate      <span class="pl-k">|</span> 173   <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Table_locks_waited         <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0     <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Table_open_cache_hits      <span class="pl-k">|</span> 5     <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Table_open_cache_misses    <span class="pl-k">|</span> 8     <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Table_open_cache_overflows <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0     <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+----------------------------+-------+
5 rows <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-c1">set</span> (0.00 sec)</pre></div>
<p>可以通过<code>Table_locks_immediate</code>和<code>Table_locks_waited</code>状态变量来分析系统上的表锁定。具体说明如下：</p>
<p><code>Table_locks_immediate</code>：产生表级锁定的次数，表示可以立即获取锁的查询次数，每立即获取锁值加1。</p>
<p><code>Table_locks_waited</code>：出现表级锁定争用而发生等待的次数（不能立即获取锁的次数，每等待一次锁值加1），此值高则说明存在较严重的表级锁争用情况。</p>
<p><strong>此外，<code>MyISAM</code>的读写锁调度是写优先，这也是<code>MyISAM</code>不适合作为主表的引擎。因为写锁后，其他线程不能进行任何操作，大量的写操作会使查询很难得到锁，从而造成永远阻塞。</strong></p>
<h1><a id="user-content-17行锁偏写" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#17行锁偏写"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>17.行锁(偏写)</h1>
<p><strong>行锁特点：</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>偏向<code>InnoDB</code>存储引擎，开销大，加锁慢；会出现死锁；锁定粒度最小，发生锁冲突的概率最低，并发度最高。</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><code>InnoDB</code>存储引擎和<code>MyISAM</code>存储引擎最大不同有两点：一是支持事务，二是采用行锁。</strong></p>
<p>事务的ACID：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>Atomicity [ˌætəˈmɪsəti] </code>。</li>
<li><code>Consistency [kənˈsɪstənsi] </code>。</li>
<li><code>Isolation [ˌaɪsəˈleɪʃn]</code>。</li>
<li><code>Durability [ˌdjʊərəˈbɪlɪti] </code>。</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-171环境准备" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#171环境准备"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>17.1.环境准备</h2>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 建表语句</span>
<span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">TABLE</span> `<span class="pl-en">test_innodb_lock</span>`(
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>a<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">INT</span>,
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>b<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">VARCHAR</span>(<span class="pl-c1">16</span>)
)ENGINE<span class="pl-k">=</span>INNODB DEFAULT CHARSET<span class="pl-k">=</span>utf8 COMMENT<span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>测试行锁<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>; 

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 插入数据</span>
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test_innodb_lock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>a<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>b<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>b2<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test_innodb_lock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>a<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>b<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>3<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test_innodb_lock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>a<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>b<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-c1">3</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>4000<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test_innodb_lock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>a<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>b<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>5000<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test_innodb_lock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>a<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>b<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-c1">5</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>6000<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test_innodb_lock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>a<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>b<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-c1">6</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>7000<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test_innodb_lock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>a<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>b<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-c1">7</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>8000<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test_innodb_lock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>a<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>b<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">VALUES</span>(<span class="pl-c1">8</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>9000<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 创建索引</span>
<span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">INDEX</span> <span class="pl-en">idx_test_a</span> <span class="pl-k">ON</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test_innodb_lock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(a);
<span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">INDEX</span> <span class="pl-en">idx_test_b</span> <span class="pl-k">ON</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test_innodb_lock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>(b);</pre></div>
<h2><a id="user-content-172行锁案例" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#172行锁案例"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>17.2.行锁案例</h2>
<blockquote>
<p>1、开启手动提交</p>
</blockquote>
<p>打开<code>SESSION1</code>和<code>SESSION2</code>两个会话，都开启手动提交。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 开启MySQL数据库的手动提交</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SET autocommit=0<span class="pl-k">;</span>
Query OK, 0 rows affected (0.00 sec)</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>2、读几知所写</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> SESSION1 </span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> SESSION1対test_innodb_lock表做写操作，但是没有commit。</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 执行修改SQL之后，查询一下test_innodb_lock表，发现数据被修改了。</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> UPDATE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test_innodb_lock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> SET <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>b<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> = <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>88<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> WHERE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>a<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> = 1<span class="pl-k">;</span>
Query OK, 1 row affected (0.00 sec)
Rows matched: 1  Changed: 1  Warnings: 0

mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SELECT <span class="pl-k">*</span> FROM <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test_innodb_lock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span>
+------+------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> a    <span class="pl-k">|</span> b    <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+------+------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span>    1 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 88   <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>    2 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 3    <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>    3 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 4000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>    4 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 5000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>    5 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 6000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>    6 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 7000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>    7 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 8000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>    8 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 9000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+------+------+
8 rows <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-c1">set</span> (0.00 sec)

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> SESSION2 </span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> SESSION2这时候来查询test_innodb_lock表。</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 发现SESSION2是读不到SESSION1未提交的数据的。</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SELECT <span class="pl-k">*</span> FROM <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test_innodb_lock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span>
+------+------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> a    <span class="pl-k">|</span> b    <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+------+------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span>    1 <span class="pl-k">|</span> b2   <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>    2 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 3    <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>    3 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 4000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>    4 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 5000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>    5 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 6000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>    6 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 7000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>    7 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 8000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span>    8 <span class="pl-k">|</span> 9000 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+------+------+
8 rows <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-c1">set</span> (0.00 se</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>3、行锁两个SESSION同时対一条记录进行写操作</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> SESSION1 対test_innodb_lock表的`a`=1这一行进行写操作，但是没有commit</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> UPDATE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test_innodb_lock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> SET <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>b<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> = <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>99<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> WHERE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>a<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> = 1<span class="pl-k">;</span>
Query OK, 1 row affected (0.00 sec)
Rows matched: 1  Changed: 1  Warnings: 0

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> SESSION2 也对test_innodb_lock表的`a`=1这一行进行写操作，但是发现阻塞了！！！</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 等SESSION1执行commit语句之后，SESSION2的SQL就会执行了</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> UPDATE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test_innodb_lock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> SET <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>b<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> = <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>asdasd<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> WHERE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>a<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> = 1<span class="pl-k">;</span>
ERROR 1205 (HY000): Lock <span class="pl-c1">wait</span> timeout exceeded<span class="pl-k">;</span> try restarting transaction</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>4、行锁两个SESSION同时对不同记录进行写操作</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> SESSION1 対test_innodb_lock表的`a`=6这一行进行写操作，但是没有commit</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> UPDATE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test_innodb_lock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> SET <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>b<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> = <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>8976<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> WHERE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>a<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> = 6<span class="pl-k">;</span>
Query OK, 1 row affected (0.00 sec)
Rows matched: 1  Changed: 1  Warnings: 0

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> SESSION2 対test_innodb_lock表的`a`=4这一行进行写操作，没有阻塞！！！</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> SESSION1和SESSION2同时对不同的行进行写操作互不影响</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> UPDATE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test_innodb_lock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> SET <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>b<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> = <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Ringo<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> WHERE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>a<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> = 4<span class="pl-k">;</span>
Query OK, 1 row affected (0.00 sec)
Rows matched: 1  Changed: 1  Warnings: 0</pre></div>
<h2><a id="user-content-173索引失效行锁变表锁" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#173索引失效行锁变表锁"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>17.3.索引失效行锁变表锁</h2>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> SESSION1 执行SQL语句，没有执行commit。</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 由于`b`字段是字符串，但是没有加单引号导致索引失效</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> UPDATE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test_innodb_lock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> SET <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>a<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> = 888 WHERE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>b<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> = 8000<span class="pl-k">;</span>
Query OK, 1 row affected, 1 warning (0.00 sec)
Rows matched: 1  Changed: 1  Warnings: 1

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> SESSION2 和SESSION1操作的并不是同一行，但是也被阻塞了？？？</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 由于SESSION1执行的SQL索引失效，导致行锁升级为表锁。</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> UPDATE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>test_innodb_lock<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> SET <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>b<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> = <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>1314<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> WHERE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>a<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> = 1<span class="pl-k">;</span>
ERROR 1205 (HY000): Lock <span class="pl-c1">wait</span> timeout exceeded<span class="pl-k">;</span> try restarting transaction</pre></div>
<h2><a id="user-content-174间隙锁的危害" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#174间隙锁的危害"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>17.4.间隙锁的危害</h2>
<blockquote>
<p>什么是间隙锁？</p>
</blockquote>
<p>当我们用范围条件而不是相等条件检索数据，并请求共享或者排他锁时，<code>InnoDB</code>会给符合条件的已有数据记录的索引项加锁，对于键值在条件范文内但并不存在的记录，叫做"间隙(GAP)"。</p>
<p><code>InnoDB</code>也会对这个"间隙"加锁，这种锁的机制就是所谓的"间隙锁"。</p>
<blockquote>
<p>间隙锁的危害</p>
</blockquote>
<p>因为<code>Query</code>执行过程中通过范围查找的话，他会锁定整个范围内所有的索引键值，即使这个键值不存在。</p>
<p>间隙锁有一个比较致命的缺点，就是**当锁定一个范围的键值后，即使某些不存在的键值也会被无辜的锁定，而造成在锁定的时候无法插入锁定键值范围内的任何数据。**在某些场景下这可能会対性能造成很大的危害。</p>
<h2><a id="user-content-175如何锁定一行" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#175如何锁定一行"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>17.5.如何锁定一行</h2>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/e5a381130dc0fdc8155bd9459dede1fc8598913dcd6aeabc7fa7b6c36d6dce24/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f323032303038303631363035303335352e706e673f782d6f73732d70726f636573733d696d6167652f77617465726d61726b2c747970655f5a6d46755a33706f5a57356e6147567064476b2c736861646f775f31302c746578745f6148523063484d364c7939696247396e4c6d4e7a5a473475626d56304c314a796157356e6231383d2c73697a655f31362c636f6c6f725f4646464646462c745f3730"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/e5a381130dc0fdc8155bd9459dede1fc8598913dcd6aeabc7fa7b6c36d6dce24/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f323032303038303631363035303335352e706e673f782d6f73732d70726f636573733d696d6167652f77617465726d61726b2c747970655f5a6d46755a33706f5a57356e6147567064476b2c736861646f775f31302c746578745f6148523063484d364c7939696247396e4c6d4e7a5a473475626d56304c314a796157356e6231383d2c73697a655f31362c636f6c6f725f4646464646462c745f3730" alt="锁定一行" data-canonical-src="https://img-blog.csdnimg.cn/2020080616050355.png?x-oss-process=image/watermark,type_ZmFuZ3poZW5naGVpdGk,shadow_10,text_aHR0cHM6Ly9ibG9nLmNzZG4ubmV0L1JyaW5nb18=,size_16,color_FFFFFF,t_70" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p><code>SELECT .....FOR UPDATE</code>在锁定某一行后，其他写操作会被阻塞，直到锁定的行被<code>COMMIT</code>。</p>
<h2><a id="user-content-176案例结论" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#176案例结论"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>17.6.案例结论</h2>
<p><code>InnoDB</code>存储引擎由于实现了行级锁定，虽然在锁定机制的实现方面所带来的性能损耗可能比表级锁定会要更高一些，但是在整体并发处理能力方面要远远优于<code>MyISAM</code>的表级锁定的。当系统并发量较高的时候，<code>InnoDB</code>的整体性能和<code>MyISAM</code>相比就会有比较明显的优势了。</p>
<p>但是，<code>InnoDB</code>的行级锁定同样也有其脆弱的一面，当我们使用不当的时候，可能会让<code>InnoDB</code>的整体性能表现不仅不能比<code>MyISAM</code>高，甚至可能会更差。</p>
<h2><a id="user-content-177行锁分析" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#177行锁分析"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>17.7.行锁分析</h2>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SHOW STATUS LIKE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>innodb_row_lock%<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span>
+-------------------------------+--------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Variable_name                 <span class="pl-k">|</span> Value  <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+-------------------------------+--------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Innodb_row_lock_current_waits <span class="pl-k">|</span> 0      <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Innodb_row_lock_time          <span class="pl-k">|</span> 124150 <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Innodb_row_lock_time_avg      <span class="pl-k">|</span> 31037  <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Innodb_row_lock_time_max      <span class="pl-k">|</span> 51004  <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Innodb_row_lock_waits         <span class="pl-k">|</span> 4      <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+-------------------------------+--------+
5 rows <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-c1">set</span> (0.00 sec)</pre></div>
<p>対各个状态量的说明如下：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>Innodb_row_lock_current_waits</code>：当前正在等待锁定的数量。</li>
<li><code>Innodb_row_lock_time</code>：从系统启动到现在锁定总时间长度（重要）。</li>
<li><code>Innodb_row_lock_time_avg</code>：每次等待所花的平均时间（重要）。</li>
<li><code>Innodb_row_lock_time_max</code>：从系统启动到现在等待最长的一次所花的时间。</li>
<li><code>Innodb_row_lock_waits</code>：系统启动后到现在总共等待的次数（重要）。</li>
</ul>
<p>尤其是当等待次数很高，而且每次等待时长也不小的时候，我们就需要分析系统中为什么会有如此多的等待，然后根据分析结果着手制定优化策略。</p>
<h1><a id="user-content-18主从复制" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#18主从复制"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>18.主从复制</h1>
<h2><a id="user-content-181复制基本原理" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#181复制基本原理"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>18.1.复制基本原理</h2>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/640beeb0ebd17d217b5d3b6902d353fab0d718cc0d674979c11cbe8e5b2275b1/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830363137303431353430312e706e673f782d6f73732d70726f636573733d696d6167652f77617465726d61726b2c747970655f5a6d46755a33706f5a57356e6147567064476b2c736861646f775f31302c746578745f6148523063484d364c7939696247396e4c6d4e7a5a473475626d56304c314a796157356e6231383d2c73697a655f31362c636f6c6f725f4646464646462c745f3730"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/640beeb0ebd17d217b5d3b6902d353fab0d718cc0d674979c11cbe8e5b2275b1/68747470733a2f2f696d672d626c6f672e6373646e696d672e636e2f32303230303830363137303431353430312e706e673f782d6f73732d70726f636573733d696d6167652f77617465726d61726b2c747970655f5a6d46755a33706f5a57356e6147567064476b2c736861646f775f31302c746578745f6148523063484d364c7939696247396e4c6d4e7a5a473475626d56304c314a796157356e6231383d2c73697a655f31362c636f6c6f725f4646464646462c745f3730" alt="主从复制" data-canonical-src="https://img-blog.csdnimg.cn/20200806170415401.png?x-oss-process=image/watermark,type_ZmFuZ3poZW5naGVpdGk,shadow_10,text_aHR0cHM6Ly9ibG9nLmNzZG4ubmV0L1JyaW5nb18=,size_16,color_FFFFFF,t_70" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p>MySQL复制过程分为三步：</p>
<ul>
<li>Master将改变记录到二进制日志(Binary Log)。这些记录过程叫做二进制日志事件，<code>Binary Log Events</code>；</li>
<li>Slave将Master的<code>Binary Log Events</code>拷贝到它的中继日志(Replay  Log);</li>
<li>Slave重做中继日志中的事件，将改变应用到自己的数据库中。MySQL复制是异步且串行化的。</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-182复制基本原则" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#182复制基本原则"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>18.2.复制基本原则</h2>
<ul>
<li>每个Slave只有一个Master。</li>
<li>每个Slave只能有一个唯一的服务器ID。</li>
<li>每个Master可以有多个Salve。</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-183一主一从配置" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#183一主一从配置"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>18.3.一主一从配置</h2>
<blockquote>
<p>1、基本要求：Master和Slave的MySQL服务器版本一致且后台以服务运行。</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 创建mysql-slave1实例</span>
docker run -p 3307:3306 --name mysql-slave1 \
-v /root/mysql-slave1/log:/var/log/mysql \
-v /root/mysql-slave1/data:/var/lib/mysql \
-v /root/mysql-slave1/conf:/etc/mysql \
-e MYSQL_ROOT_PASSWORD=333 \
-d mysql:5.7</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>2、主从配置都是配在[mysqld]节点下，都是小写</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Master配置</span>
[mysqld]
server-id=1 <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 必须</span>
log-bin=/var/lib/mysql/mysql-bin <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 必须</span>
read-only=0
binlog-ignore-db=mysql</pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Slave配置</span>
[mysqld]
server-id=2 <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 必须</span>
log-bin=/var/lib/mysql/mysql-bin</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>3、Master配置</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 1、GRANT REPLICATION SLAVE ON *.* TO 'username'@'从机IP地址' IDENTIFIED BY 'password';</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> GRANT REPLICATION SLAVE ON <span class="pl-k">*</span>.<span class="pl-k">*</span> TO <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>zhangsan<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>@<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>172.18.0.3<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> IDENTIFIED BY <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>123456<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span>
Query OK, 0 rows affected, 1 warning (0.01 sec)

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 2、刷新命令</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> FLUSH PRIVILEGES<span class="pl-k">;</span>
Query OK, 0 rows affected (0.00 sec)

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 3、记录下File和Position</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 每次配从机的时候都要SHOW MASTER STATUS;查看最新的File和Position</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SHOW MASTER STATUS<span class="pl-k">;</span>
+------------------+----------+--------------+------------------+-------------------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> File             <span class="pl-k">|</span> Position <span class="pl-k">|</span> Binlog_Do_DB <span class="pl-k">|</span> Binlog_Ignore_DB <span class="pl-k">|</span> Executed_Gtid_Set <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+------------------+----------+--------------+------------------+-------------------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> mysql-bin.000001 <span class="pl-k">|</span>      602 <span class="pl-k">|</span>              <span class="pl-k">|</span> mysql            <span class="pl-k">|</span>                   <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+------------------+----------+--------------+------------------+-------------------+
1 row <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-c1">set</span> (0.00 sec)</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>4、Slave从机配置</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>CHANGE MASTER TO MASTER_HOST=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>172.18.0.4<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
MASTER_USER=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>zhangsan<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
MASTER_PASSWORD=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>123456<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
MASTER_LOG_FILE=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>mysql-bin.File的编号<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
MASTER_LOG_POS=Position的最新值<span class="pl-k">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 1、使用用户名密码登录进Master</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> CHANGE MASTER TO MASTER_HOST=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>172.18.0.4<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
    -<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> MASTER_USER=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>zhangsan<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
    -<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> MASTER_PASSWORD=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>123456<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
    -<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> MASTER_LOG_FILE=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>mysql-bin.000001<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
    -<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> MASTER_LOG_POS=602<span class="pl-k">;</span>
Query OK, 0 rows affected, 2 warnings (0.02 sec)

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 2、开启Slave从机的复制</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> START SLAVE<span class="pl-k">;</span>
Query OK, 0 rows affected (0.00 sec)

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 3、查看Slave状态</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Slave_IO_Running 和 Slave_SQL_Running 必须同时为Yes 说明主从复制配置成功！</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SHOW SLAVE STATUS<span class="pl-cce">\G</span>
<span class="pl-k">***************************</span> 1. row <span class="pl-k">***************************</span>
               Slave_IO_State: Waiting <span class="pl-k">for</span> master to send event <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Slave待命状态</span>
                  Master_Host: 172.18.0.4
                  Master_User: zhangsan
                  Master_Port: 3306
                Connect_Retry: 60
              Master_Log_File: mysql-bin.000001
          Read_Master_Log_Pos: 602
               Relay_Log_File: b030ad25d5fe-relay-bin.000002
                Relay_Log_Pos: 320
        Relay_Master_Log_File: mysql-bin.000001
             Slave_IO_Running: Yes  
            Slave_SQL_Running: Yes
              Replicate_Do_DB: 
          Replicate_Ignore_DB: 
           Replicate_Do_Table: 
       Replicate_Ignore_Table: 
      Replicate_Wild_Do_Table: 
  Replicate_Wild_Ignore_Table: 
                   Last_Errno: 0
                   Last_Error: 
                 Skip_Counter: 0
          Exec_Master_Log_Pos: 602
              Relay_Log_Space: 534
              Until_Condition: None
               Until_Log_File: 
                Until_Log_Pos: 0
           Master_SSL_Allowed: No
           Master_SSL_CA_File: 
           Master_SSL_CA_Path: 
              Master_SSL_Cert: 
            Master_SSL_Cipher: 
               Master_SSL_Key: 
        Seconds_Behind_Master: 0
Master_SSL_Verify_Server_Cert: No
                Last_IO_Errno: 0
                Last_IO_Error: 
               Last_SQL_Errno: 0
               Last_SQL_Error: 
  Replicate_Ignore_Server_Ids: 
             Master_Server_Id: 1
                  Master_UUID: bd047557-b20c-11ea-9961-0242ac120002
             Master_Info_File: /var/lib/mysql/master.info
                    SQL_Delay: 0
          SQL_Remaining_Delay: NULL
      Slave_SQL_Running_State: Slave has <span class="pl-c1">read</span> all relay log<span class="pl-k">;</span> waiting <span class="pl-k">for</span> more updates
           Master_Retry_Count: 86400
                  Master_Bind: 
      Last_IO_Error_Timestamp: 
     Last_SQL_Error_Timestamp: 
               Master_SSL_Crl: 
           Master_SSL_Crlpath: 
           Retrieved_Gtid_Set: 
            Executed_Gtid_Set: 
                Auto_Position: 0
         Replicate_Rewrite_DB: 
                 Channel_Name: 
           Master_TLS_Version: 
1 row <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-c1">set</span> (0.00 sec)</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>5、测试主从复制</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Master创建数据库</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> create database test_replication<span class="pl-k">;</span>
Query OK, 1 row affected (0.01 sec)

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Slave查询数据库</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> show databases<span class="pl-k">;</span>
+--------------------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> Database           <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+--------------------+
<span class="pl-k">|</span> information_schema <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> mysql              <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> performance_schema <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> sys                <span class="pl-k">|</span>
<span class="pl-k">|</span> test_replication   <span class="pl-k">|</span>
+--------------------+
5 rows <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-c1">set</span> (0.00 sec)</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>6、停止主从复制功能</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 1、停止Slave</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> STOP SLAVE<span class="pl-k">;</span>
Query OK, 0 rows affected (0.00 sec)

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 2、重新配置主从</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> MASTER_LOG_FILE 和 MASTER_LOG_POS一定要根据最新的数据来配</span>
mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> CHANGE MASTER TO MASTER_HOST=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>172.18.0.4<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
    -<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> MASTER_USER=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>zhangsan<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
    -<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> MASTER_PASSWORD=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>123456<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
    -<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> MASTER_LOG_FILE=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>mysql-bin.000001<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
    -<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> MASTER_LOG_POS=797<span class="pl-k">;</span>
Query OK, 0 rows affected, 2 warnings (0.01 sec)

mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> START SLAVE<span class="pl-k">;</span>
Query OK, 0 rows affected (0.00 sec)

mysql<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> SHOW SLAVE STATUS<span class="pl-cce">\G</span>
<span class="pl-k">***************************</span> 1. row <span class="pl-k">***************************</span>
